[P Security Team Kills Fifteen Bandits

Squad Leader Li immediately ordered his troops to open fire. The bandits also returned fire. After about two hours of fighting, Squad Leader Li led his troops in a fierce charge, and the bandits were unable to resist and scattered and fled. Ding Waizu and fifteen bandits were killed on the spot, and three Mauser pistols and one rifle were captured.

[P Entire Carpentry Industry Goes on Strike

At Xu Shunchang Carpentry in Xiaoguqiao, West Gate of this city, during the defunct Dragon Boat Festival, worker Chen was fired. All of Chen's back wages for one day had not been paid. The workers were dissatisfied. On the 22nd, all the workers went on strike. The owners immediately reported to the county government to strictly prohibit the riots. The county government posted notice of strict prohibition and ordered the Public Security Bureau to investigate the facts. Team Leader Hu of the investigation team of the bureau investigated the strike situation, which was roughly as described above. Chief Chen Hongji, together with the county party headquarters, has been properly mediating, and ordered all the workers to resume work first, pending a solution.

Shaoxing

[P Provincial Order to Collect Defense Corps Funds

The funds for the Shaoxing Defense Corps were previously approved to be collected with the grain tax until the 19th year. Now, because there are no other funds that can be raised, the Defense Committee decided to submit a document to the province through the county to request that the funds be collected for one year under the land tax offset funds for the 20th year. Yesterday, the province issued an order approving the request.

Ningbo

[P Hurricane Capsizes Robber Boat, Drowning Many Bandits

Four men from Yin County, Ni Yangsheng, Xie Acai, Tong A'er, and Huang Agen, were engaged in the pig trade. The day before yesterday, they bought more than 170 piglets from Jiangyin, Jiangsu Province, and hired a boat to sell them. When they passed Hengshanxia, Yuyao, they were suddenly surrounded by two robber boats with more than 30 bandits. Because there was nothing to rob in the boat, they tied up Ni Yangsheng, Xie Asheng, and Tong A'er, and let Huang Agen return to Ningbo to notify their families to prepare money for ransom. The two robber boats hijacked the pig boat and stopped in place to wait for news. Unexpectedly, a hurricane suddenly arose that day, capsizing one of the robber boats, drowning the pig trader Ni Yangsheng, seven bandits, and three boatmen. Also, near the coast of Xinpu, Yuyao, a robber boat capsized the other day. When the robber boat capsized, it was seen by the boat supported by Zhou Laoyuan in the nearby East San Village. He rescued seven pirates. Twenty-two people drowned. Many firearms were also recovered. The rescued pirates, after landing, feared being arrested and scattered and fled.

Xuzhou

[P Examination of the Case of Murdering One's Husband

In the case of Zheng Zhangshi and her adulterer, Min Guangyu, plotting to murder her husband, Zheng Zhongren, to death in Liuquan, this county, the trial official, Li Weiyuan, opened the court for detailed trial at 4:00 p.m. yesterday. According to the adulterer, Min Guangyu, Zheng Zhongren was strangled to death by Zheng Zhangshi on the night of the ninth day of the first month of this year. I took the body out, and it was only discovered on the day of peace. Interrogated, Zheng Zhangshi's confession was consistent. By 6:00 p.m., Trial Official Li ordered him to be taken into custody. To be cautious, he led the officials to conduct a detailed examination at 5:00 a.m. today (the 23rd) to provide evidence for legal action.

Ning County Elementary School Graduates' Joint Examination 140

In order to understand the achievements of sixth-grade graduates of elementary schools, the Education Bureau of Jiangning County specially organized a senior graduate joint examination committee. The procedures for the joint examination had been prepared long ago and were scheduled to be held on June 22. On that day, all senior graduates of the county first gathered at the County Education Association, preparing to try together. More than one hundred people arrived. The examination subjects were divided into four subjects: Party Ideology, Language, Arithmetic, and Common Sense. Each examination paper was prepared by the Education Bureau in advance. The face of the paper was affixed with a floating ticket, the seats were numbered, and the back of the paper was sealed. After calling the roll and distributing the papers, each student entered the examination hall in an orderly manner and sat down in order. Administrative personnel from the Education Bureau attended the examination, with strict security and orderly procedures. The evaluation of the examination results has now been entrusted to special personnel. As soon as the evaluation is completed, it will be announced to the schools. Students who have completed the junior course will also be jointly examined in separate districts soon. It is planned that supervisors and other personnel will be sent to supervise the examination separately to show solemnity.

Xinhua Art College

Ginling Women's College 147

Ginling Women's College held its thirteenth graduation ceremony at 10:00 a.m. on the 24th. Hundreds of guests attended. After playing music and reading Sun Yat-sen's will, President Wu Yifang delivered a speech, stating that the school has been thriving in recent years in all aspects. The increase in the number of students is self-evident, and the expansion of school buildings, the improvement of equipment, and the increase of course programs have also broken previous records. However, all of this is not enough to measure the true value of a school. The most important point is to see how well the graduates serve society after leaving school. According to statistics, there are a total of 171 graduates from the school, the largest number of whom serve in the education field, accounting for 71.3% of the total. The political sector accounts for 2.3%, social undertakings 7.8%, authors 1.7%, and those who continue their studies at home and abroad 14.6%. Their service locations range from Liaoning in the north to Sichuan in the west, and from Yunnan to Guangdong in the south, totaling 13 provinces. Among the 18 graduates this year, in addition to three who intend to continue their studies, the rest have been invited by various parties, with 11 teaching, three handling educational administration, and one engaging in social work. Sun Benwen, director of the Higher Education Department of the Ministry of Education, then delivered a speech, with the main points being: (1) Continue to study advanced knowledge; (2) Develop national undertakings; (3) Promote inherent culture; (4) Cultivate noble character. Luo Jialun, director of the Academic Affairs Department of the Central Political School, and Ms. Zhang Mojun, member of the Legislative Yuan, then gave speeches. After the speeches, diplomas were awarded.

Physician Chen Bangdian Returns Home After Completing Studies 149

Medical Doctor Chen Bangdian, style name Mengqiao, is from Jiading County, Jiangsu Province. He is the eldest son of Chen Zhongda, the current Magistrate of Jiading County. After graduating from the Medical Department of St. John's University, he served as a doctor at Tongren Hospital and as the Director of Medical Affairs at the Shanghai Epidemic Hospital. In the summer of 1918, he traveled to the United States to study at the Medical College of the University of Pennsylvania, specializing in obstetrics. He has now completed his studies and returned to China, arriving in Shanghai on the 9th of this month. Xicheng Primary School Provides Guidance for Further Education and Employment 153

In order to facilitate the further education and employment of this year's graduates, the Municipal Xicheng Primary School on Penglai Road has established a Guidance Committee for Further Education and Employment. Since its establishment, the committee has not only conducted surveys and collected opinions, but also invited Yang Weiyu, the principal of the China Vocational School, and Pan Yangyao, the director of the Shanghai Vocational Introduction Office, to give lectures at the school on the morning of the 25th. Yang Weiyu spoke on "Why Study and How to Be a Person," while Pan Yangyao spoke on the differences between Chinese and foreign vocational circles and the common misconceptions about the word "study," emphasizing that professions have no high or low status and that one should strive to make the most of one's abilities. He also proposed points to consider when pursuing further education and employment, generally saying that one should not be hasty, careless, or impatient in pursuing further education, and that one should not dislike humble jobs, fear hardship, or be concerned about compensation in seeking employment.

The Increasingly Tense World Tennis Championships 160

丨Only Sixteen Players Remain in Men's Singles丨Two Japanese Players Eliminated丨

丨Men's Doubles First Week Begins丨Only Two Groups Compete丨

丨Women's Singles - Unexpected Results丨Spanish Champion Loses丨

London, 24th (Report) 161

With low cloud cover and occasional showers, today's Wimbledon tennis matches were only held on the Centre Court and Court No. 1. The men's singles has entered the third week of competition, with only sixteen players remaining. The atmosphere is becoming increasingly tense.

Two More Japanese Players Eliminated 162

At the start of the third week, two Japanese players were eliminated. Kawachi and Miki both lost. Only Sato Jiro remains. France's Boussus defeated Kawachi 6-3, 6-3, 6-4. France's Borotra defeated Miki 6-4, 6-1, 6-2. Boussus's chops and endurance overcame Kawachi's long rallies. Boussus often hit the ball to both sides. At the beginning of the second set, Boussus took a 4-1 lead. Kawachi relied entirely on his serve, but it was to no avail. Miki's battle was also tragic, defending the baseline with long rallies, but he was always blocked and smashed by Borotra at the net. Miki's backhand gave Borotra some trouble. In the third set, he repeatedly faulted on his second serve. In the end, he still lost decisively.

Indian Player's Strategy Fails 163

Japan's Sato Jiro's victory over India's Mohan was very interesting. The score was 6-3, 6-2, 6-3. Sato's fierce serve was initially blocked by Mohan, but his net play was unstoppable. In the second set, Mohan changed shoes due to the slippery ground, but Sato did not care and continued to run as he pleased. Mohan also dropped his racket, but it was to no avail. Sato won very easily.

Austin Decisively Defeats French Swordsman 164

France's Borotra is one of the "Four Musketeers," but England's Austin decisively defeated him. The victory came very easily. Austin is widely believed to be a contender for the final. The score was 6-3, 6-4, 6-0.

Loss of Lott Disappoints 165

American player Lott lost to England's Lee, and Lee won without difficulty. It was disappointing. The score was 7-5, 7-5, 7-5. However, Shields and Van Ryn both won decisively.

Argentina Completely Fails 166

Argentina's last hope, Castillo, was defeated by England's Hughes.

Germany Still Has One Player 167

Germany still has one player left, who defeated England's Kingsly, a member of the Davis Cup team, yesterday.

Men's Doubles Competition Begins 168

The men's doubles competition began today. Two Indian players and the Sato-Tawarazumio team won.

In the women's singles, Spain's Franaise, who had high hopes, unexpectedly lost to England's Longnet in the third week. The score was 6-3, 6-3. This was a great surprise. Former King Alfonso of Spain was present at the match and was deeply saddened by Franaise's misfortune. He kissed her hand to console her when he met her. German champion Olsen entered the fourth week, defeating Egypt's Alexandrov.

Local News

Chen Zhaoying Discusses the Current Situation 173

Suppression of Communists in Jiangxi - Simultaneous Military and Political Advances

Fujian Province's Finances Will Be Unsustainable

Guangdong's Troubles Will Not Lead to Military Conflict

Chen Will Go to Fujian to Comfort Lu and Liu

According to Riri Fu, Central Committee member Chen Zhaoying was ordered by Chairman Chiang to go to Fujian to comfort Generals Liu Heding and Lu Xingbang, and to discuss urgent plans such as preventing the Communists from fleeing into Fujian. He is currently staying in Shanghai for a few days. Yesterday, Chen made an important speech to a Riri Fu reporter regarding the current situation. The details are as follows:

Suppression of the Communists Plan 174

Commander-in-Chief Chiang's suppression of the Communists in Jiangxi aims to completely eliminate them in the shortest possible time. The plan has been divided into two routes, military and political, to be carried out simultaneously.

Central Committee Members Depart 175

In this suppression of the Communists, not only will all the generals and soldiers lead their troops on a long expedition, but also civil officials will bear important missions. Before Commander-in-Chief Chiang went to Jiangxi, he stipulated a plan that all Central Committee members, except for the elderly who remained in Nanjing, would set off for various places. Their sole task is to supervise and order the local just gentlemen to unite and work together, using local forces as a backup for the government. Since the Communist bandits ravaged the area, the respected elders in the area have been influenced by the Communist bandits, believing that all the respected figures in the area, regardless of their character, must be regarded as local tyrants and evil gentry, causing the local gentry not to dare to show their faces. The social center of gravity has therefore been overthrown. The task of the current departure of the Central Committee members is to judge right and wrong in the local area, and to distinguish between black and white. If they are indeed respected figures in the village, no matter what, they must be invited to come out and take on local work and fulfill a part of their responsibility for the local area. If they are local bullies, they should be eradicated, so as to restore the local center of gravity.

Fujian Province Finances 176

Fujian Province's financial difficulties have reached an extreme point. This is because the local area is barren and revenue is very small. Recently, even the provincial government's food expenses have been difficult to pay, which is heartbreaking to say. If the central government does not provide a follow-up solution, it will inevitably become unsustainable. Recently, although 500,000 treasury bonds have been issued, it is only a drop in the bucket and only provides temporary relief. It is still not a long-term solution, and the merchants and people are unable to bear the burden due to poverty. Before the Fifth Plenary Session, Chairman Yang Shuzhuang went to Nanjing and had a discussion with Finance Minister Song. It has been heard that there is some progress.

Guangdong Matters 177

Chen also told the Riri Fu reporter that the Guangdong matters will definitely not lead to military conflict. It is entirely a party dispute and must of course be resolved within the party. Zhang Puquan's trip to Guangdong to mediate has been quite successful. The central government is like an older brother, and Guangdong and Chen are like younger brothers. If the older brother makes a slight mistake, the younger brothers should do their best to persuade him. If the younger brothers have irregular actions, the older brother should also correct them. In short, this matter can be understood by each other, and it will not lead to major conflict.

Current Situation of Communists in Jiangxi 178

The Communists in Jiangxi are most rampant under Zhu, Mao, Peng, He, etc. However, the people have been tired of the chaos for a long time. The Communist bandits initially used the beautiful names of not paying grain and not paying taxes to lure the ignorant people. As a result, the masses responded. After occupying a place, they established Soviet governments everywhere, repeatedly distributing rice to the people, and the people had no choice but to obey. Their losses were indeed immeasurable compared to paying grain and taxes. Therefore, the people who have been ravaged by the Communist bandits all said that they would rather pay grain and taxes than be ruled by the Communist bandits. They are now eager for the arrival of the central army. Therefore, this suppression of the Communists will definitely be able to clarify the situation in the shortest possible time.

Date of Departure for Fujian 179

The reporter then asked Chen when he would go to Fujian. Chen replied that he was scheduled to go to Fujian next Wednesday on the Wanchang ship. The task there, in addition to comforting Liu and Lu, would be to go to Zhang Zhen's place and discuss the plan to prevent the Communists. Because the Communist bandits in Jiangxi, after hearing that the central government was personally征, could not help but be胆寒. They have now shrunk their range, and one part has fled into Fujian, and one part has fallen into Zixi and fled to Zhejiang. Therefore, it is necessary to discuss with Liu and others the plan to jointly prevent the spread of the Communist bandits, and to prevent them from crossing the Zhejiang province's Leichi. Otherwise, it will not be a minor problem. It is heard that Chen discussed various issues in Fujian Province with Navy Minister Yang Shuzhuang yesterday afternoon. At that time, he may have to go to Fujian with Yang at the same time.

Chen Shaokuan's Remarks 180

According to Riri Fu, Navy Acting Minister Chen Shaokuan arrived in Shanghai from Nanjing yesterday morning. A Riri Fu reporter specially visited Chen at the Jiangnan Shipyard and asked about the navy's plans and various issues regarding the current situation. He gave detailed answers. The main points are as follows:

Two New Large Warships Built 181

For the sake of consolidating the maritime defenses, in January of this year, the Ministry sent Chief of General Affairs Li Shijia to Japan to order a 3,000-ton warship from the Harima Shipyard, costing 4.23 million Japanese yen. It is now named Ninghai. The construction project is quite rapid. It is scheduled to be launched in Japan on Double Ten Day this year. I will personally attend the ceremony at that time. It is expected to be fully completed around April of next year and will be shipped to China for use. Another Pinghai warship is being built at the Jiangnan Shipyard, the same size as the ship ordered in Japan. The construction materials and hull drawings have all been completed. The keel is scheduled to be laid on the 28th of this month (i.e., Sunday), and it will also be completed in the winter of next year.

Fujian Province Is as Peaceful as Ever 182

Because the territory of Fujian Province is a gathering of mountains and forests, it has always been a breeding ground for bandits. Peng Dehuai's bandits fled into Fujian Province from the Jiangxi border a month ago and had some contact with Liu Heding's division, but they were quickly suppressed. What is being spread outside is not true. The maritime defenses of Fujian Province are now exceptionally strong. There are currently warships such as Hai Rong and Ying Rui distributed in the Majiang and Zhongzhou areas. All parts of the province are as peaceful as ever.

Yang Plans to Go to Hangzhou for Quiet Recuperation 183

Minister Yang Shuzhuang, due to years of heavy administrative duties, has been working hard, resulting in the recurrence of his old cough with blood disease. Now that all the finances of Fujian Province have been handled properly, and the provincial committee members Chen Peikun, etc., have all returned to Fujian, there are no more difficult problems in the Fujian Province administration. Yang plans to take the opportunity to go to Hangzhou for recuperation in order to restore his health.

Continuing to Recruit Naval Students 184

Since the construction of the Xiangshan Naval Academy began, the foundation work has been completed. Formal construction will begin in the coming days, with an estimated cost of around 100,000 yuan. It is expected to be completed at this time next year, and then 300-400 naval students will be recruited in order to train talents for the Chinese Navy. The 96 new students recruited the other day have now been sent to the Mawei Naval Academy, with a five-year graduation period. In the future, they may transfer to the Xiangshan New Military Academy.

According to the National News Agency, Navy Vice Minister and Jiangnan Shipyard Director Chen Shaokuan originally planned to depart with Chairman Chiang, but since Chiang went directly to Nanchang, he did not go with him. He returned to Shanghai by train yesterday. A reporter met him at the shipyard and conducted the following interview: (Q) Will Minister Yang return to Fujian? (A) Undecided. (Q) Feng Yipei has passed away. It is said that Yu Jishi will fill the position of Guard Division Commander. Have you heard of this? (A) Commander Feng has passed away due to overwork, which is deeply regrettable. I was not in Nanjing when the decision of who would take over his vacant position was made, so I do not know. (Q) When will the remaining torpedo boats in Shanghai conduct maneuvers in Xiangshan? (A) The torpedo boat fleet anchored in Shanghai port, consisting of eight ships including Yuzhang, Hupeng, Hu'e, Huying, Husun, Chenzi, Zhangzi, and Liezi, all set sail together at 6:20 AM this morning. Commander Zeng Yiding was on board the Yuzhang. The Jiankang and Suzi torpedo boats need some more repairs and will follow at a later date. The maneuvers are scheduled for two or three weeks, after which they will return to their posts. (Q) How was the trial run of the Ziqiang warship today? (A) The Navy's Ziqiang warship was converted from the Jianwei warship. Construction began on January 15th of this year, lasting only six months. It set sail for the Minhang area at 7:00 AM yesterday for trials. The average speed at its peak was 15.5 nautical miles. The hull is sturdy, and it is agile in forward and reverse. After the trial, it returned to Gaochang Temple at 11:30 AM to await assignment. This ship and the Datong warship, formerly known as Jianan, which was converted last year, are sister ships. The Datong took 12 months and cost over 400,000 yuan to complete successfully. Now, the Ziqiang's repair time and cost are only half that of the Datong, but the results are even better. (Q) When will you return to Nanjing? (A) After I have taken care of the matters at hand, I will also have to go to Xiangshan, first to inspect the naval academy being built there, and secondly to observe the torpedo boat fleet's maneuvers. (Q) Which warship will you take to Ningbo? (A) It will be the Yixian warship, which is about to return to duty. The internal work on the Yixian will be completed soon, and it will set sail at the latest on July 1st. After the inspection is complete, I will return directly to Nanjing. With that, I took my leave.

Zhang Xueliang Recovering from Illness, Will Leave Hospital Soon 185

Wu Tiecheng and Zhang Xueming Telegraph Mayor Zhang

Complexion very good. Body temperature and pulse are no different from those of ordinary people. Even ate a bowl of porridge this morning. Illness has been cured. Waiting quietly, and then he will be discharged from the hospital. Know this, and I am grateful. Your brother, Wu Tiecheng, bows. (1) To Shanghai Mayor Zhang Yuejun, respectfully: Your esteemed telegram has been received with respect. The Deputy Commander has now recovered. Body temperature and pulse are no different from those of ordinary people. Appetite is increasing daily. Spirit is very good. Physique is healthier. Mr. Pittman Arrived in Shanghai the Night Before Last 189

U.S. Envoy Johnson Visited Him Yesterday for Talks

He Will Leave Shanghai for Home Early Next Month

U.S. Senator Pittman, who came to China earlier to investigate silver prices, and his wife, arrived in Shanghai from Tianjin the night before last (the 24th) at approximately 11:00 PM. Yesterday afternoon at 4:20 PM, the U.S. Minister to China, Mr. Johnson, paid a special visit to the Cathay Hotel on the Bund for a meeting lasting about 30 minutes. It is said that Mr. Pittman will leave Shanghai to return home early next month.

According to the Continental Daily News, after returning to Shanghai from Beiping last night, U.S. Senator Pittman told people that an international silver conference would certainly be convened soon. He strongly supports the U.S. President's proposal to postpone war debt repayments and will fully support it, as he has long held this view and even has more progressive proposals. The gold and silver problems of the world must be resolved, and especially should be resolved quickly. He does not want to set a silver price or a gold-silver ratio, but only to agree on a method of relief so that we are not again fooled by a lack of a definitive method. Of the bankers and financiers he met on his way in Beijing and Pingjin, 90% supported the international silver conference as the only way to alleviate the current crisis. Senator Smoot in Washington is no longer as eager to hold an informal meeting as he used to be, because in the coming weeks, many people will change their attitude towards the silver conference. Empty words are useless. If there is no meeting with executive power, we might as well remain silent. Today, people in the world no longer regard local conditions as more important than the global economic downturn. There are three main reasons for the global economic downturn: (1) Uneven distribution of gold currency, (2) Inability to obtain gold currency, and (3) Frequent destruction of silver coins. India's failure to join other countries in seeking relief has made the precarious situation even more profound. India is the main cause of the oversupply of silver, which makes it impossible for other silver-producing countries to stop production.

Six organizations, including the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Bankers' Association, the International Trade Association, and the International Chamber of Commerce branch, met yesterday to discuss welcome arrangements. They have agreed to hold a public banquet for Mr. Pittman at the Bankers' Association on the 30th of this month. At the same time, they are preparing to study Mr. Pittman's findings from his recent trip to the north and discuss the procedures for convening an international silver conference.

World Peace Society Appoints Wang Jingqi as Honorary Member 190

In 1925, the World Peace Promotion Society was established in Switzerland. The supporters of the society are all well-known figures from various countries, such as former French President Poincaré, the convener of the conference Kellogg, former Foreign Minister Stresemann, British Prime Minister Chamberlain, French Foreign Minister Briand, Austrian Prime Minister Seipel, Belgian Queen Elisabeth, academic giants Madame Curie, Einstein, Edison, Marconi (inventor of the radio antenna), de Forest (inventor of the radio vacuum tube), etc. Oil magnate Rockefeller is also among them. Recently, the Presidium of the Society unanimously decided at a general meeting to appoint Mr. Wang Jingqi, the former Chinese Minister to Belgium and current President of Labour University, as an honorary member of the Society. A formal letter has been sent to Mr. Wang.

The Navigation Administration Bureau Begins Operations Today 191

Formally Moving into the Bureau's Address at No. 6 Sichuan Road

The Shanghai Navigation Administration Bureau, which was established by the Ministry of Communications, has been fully prepared since Director Xi Dingmo reported on its preparations. It will formally move into the bureau's address at No. 6 Sichuan Road today and begin operations. It will be formally established on July 1. According to Director Xi's statement to a reporter from the New Voice News Agency yesterday regarding the internal organization and the preparation of branch offices, the details are recorded separately below.

Internal Organization of the Bureau 192

The Navigation Administration Bureau is divided into two sections. The first section is responsible for general affairs such as accounting and general administration. The second section is responsible for specialized affairs such as ship inspection, registration, and measurement. There is a technical office with one director and eight technicians to assist the director in handling specialized work matters. There is also a secretary to handle various documents.

Announcement of Staff 193

The bureau's staff has been officially announced, including Secretary Yao Zhaozhi, Head of the First Section Jiang Zumin, Head of the Second Section (concurrently held by the Director), Head of the Technical Office Zhu Tiankui, and Technicians Zhu Tiankui, Cao Shoulian, Zhou Houkun, Huang Shaosan, Xu Shipu, Qin Jiyun, Meng Muzhuang, Ding Yanling, and eleven others.

Preparing Branch Offices 194

The Shanghai Navigation Administration Bureau's management area includes the three provinces of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui. The Wuhu area of Anhui originally had a ship inspection office. Since the Ministry of Communications announced the establishment of the Shanghai Navigation Administration Bureau, it sent representatives to contact the Shanghai Bureau. Yesterday, the Bureau received an order from the Ministry of Communications to immediately prepare branch offices in necessary places in the three provinces to facilitate operations. Therefore, Director Xi decided to set up branch offices in Zhenjiang in Jiangsu, Wuhu in Anhui, and Ningbo in Zhejiang, starting today, so that management can be more closely managed.

Handover Situation 195

As for the progress of the Navigation Administration Bureau taking over the ship inspection and registration section of the Jianghai Customs, the Ministry of Communications has contacted the Ministry of Finance and reached an agreement. Now, it is only waiting for the official reply from the Ministry of Finance to take over, approximately on July 1.

The Ziqiang Warship Conducted Sea Trials Yesterday 196

Scheduled to Conduct Cannon Tests and Raise Flags to Rejoin the Fleet on July 1

The naval warship Ziqiang, which was rebuilt from the abandoned warship Jianwei, has been under construction for half a year. Now, the entire project has been completed and it has been assigned to the Second Fleet as a cruiser. The Ministry has appointed Qiu Shizhong as the captain and Lin Qi as the deputy captain. Yesterday (the 25th) at 7:00 AM, Deputy Captain Lin Qi and Yu Jianfu, Deputy Director of the Shipbuilding Section, led the warship away from the port and sailed to Longhua Minhang for its first sea trial. It returned at 11:00 AM. It is reported that the sea trial results showed that the speed and efficiency were better than previous trials of warships such as Datong. It is also learned that the warship is scheduled to sail to Wusongkou on July 1 for cannon tests and raise flags to rejoin the fleet.

The Dispute Between Chinese and Foreign Vessels on the Sichuan River is Intensifying

Chinese Ships on the Upper Yangtze River Cease Operations

Yichang-Chongqing Chinese Ships Not Sailing 197

Since the 5th of this month, foreign merchant ships joined the Merchant Shipping Association, obtained transportation rights, and announced a doubling of freight rates. When foreign ships of British, Japanese, and American origin drastically reduced their freight rates, Sichuan merchants refused to load goods because Chinese ships refused to agree to price reductions. After the 6th of this month, Sichuan merchants could not bear the exploitation of foreign ships, and requested that the eight Chinese ships reduce their freight rates to counteract the foreign merchants. After discussions, the Chinese ships recognized that they were financially weak and could not compete with the oppression of foreign merchants. They refused the merchants' requests and decided to abandon sailing between Yichang and Chongqing. Chinese ships on the Yichang-Chongqing route have completely stopped operations.

Foreign Ships Further Reduce Freight Rates 198

From June 6, the freight rate for Yichang-Chongqing cotton yarn increased from two taels per piece to six taels. The freight rate for general merchandise increased to 30 taels per ton. Merchants in Yichang and Chongqing were shocked by this notice and held an emergency meeting, unanimously rejecting these freight rates. They also opposed all eleven measures announced by the various foreign ships, such as direct-run ships and half-loaded ships. The Sichuan General Chamber of Commerce and other organizations published reasons for their opposition. On the 16th, British, Japanese, and American foreign merchants also held an emergency meeting and decided to temporarily reduce the Yichang-Chongqing freight rate by one-third, allowing a charge of four taels per piece. The freight rate for cotton yarn and general merchandise was also reduced to 20 taels per ton to ease the opposition of Sichuan merchants and consolidate the foothold of Sichuan river shipping. They also agreed to cancel the previously set eleven measures.

Chinese Ships Change Route to Yichang 199

Two Chinese ships on the Sichuan River have already ceased operations. The remaining ships decided to retreat and avoid the upper reaches section, which foreign merchants are fully operating and seizing. Chinese ships will not go there automatically and will change their route to below Yichang and direct to Shanghai. After the decision, the freight rates on this route were also reduced together. The freight rate for foreign cloth was usually 8 taels, 3 mace, and 5 candareens per piece, but is now changed to 6 taels and 4 mace. The freight rate for cotton yarn was usually 7 taels, 7 mace, and 4 candareens per piece, but is now changed to 5 taels and 9 mace and 5 candareens. The freight rate for other miscellaneous items is reduced by 30%. Therefore, the upper reaches of the Yangtze River are completely dominated by foreign ships.

The China National Aviation Corporation is preparing the Wanzhou-Chongqing air route to directly connect the Shanghai-Chengdu line in the shortest possible time. American Aircraft Shipped 201

The company received a telegram from the American Sikorsky Aircraft Factory on the 23rd, stating that four fixed-wing aircraft and seven new engines have been shipped from the United States, loaded in New York, transported across the northwestern United States to Seattle, and then shipped by the Pacific Line to

China. It is expected that the new aircraft and parts will arrive in Shanghai around the 20th.

Wanzhou-Chongqing Station Preparation 202

When engineer Chustead and his team transported the radio station to Wanzhou, they inspected the Jiangbian area of Wanzhou on the 21st to set up a floating pontoon landing area. The next day, they inspected the military airfield in Chongqing and contacted the military authorities in both places to prepare for the establishment of an airport. They have received permission from the authorities in Wanzhou and Chongqing, and Mr. Chustead has reported to the company.

Opening Soon 204

When the world aviator Lindbergh arrives in Shanghai at the end of July, he will be asked to conduct a test flight first and provide guidance.

News on the Case of a Western Constable Shooting a Chinese Policeman in the West of Shanghai Yesterday 205

Officials Were Dispatched Yesterday to Negotiate

All Sectors Rallied to Provide Assistance

After a Western constable from the Haig Road Police Station in Xujiahui shot and seriously injured police officer Kong Qingfeng on the 24th of this month at 2:00 PM, he was sent to the Red Cross Hospital, as reported in yesterday's newspaper. Since the incident occurred, all organizations have been extremely indignant and have convened meetings to discuss countermeasures and send representatives to express their condolences. The situation yesterday is recorded below.

Dispatching Officials to Negotiate 206

Yesterday morning at 10:00 AM, Director Chen of the Municipal Public Security Bureau sent Secretary and Head of the Foreign Affairs Section Hong Qijun, and then personally went to the Police Department of the Public Concession to negotiate with Chief Superintendent Everson and requested four things: (1) Compensation for medical and pharmaceutical expenses for the injured policeman, (2) A formal apology to the government and official authorities, (3) A guarantee that such unfortunate incidents will not happen again in the future, (4) In the future, personnel from the concession police and Chinese and Western detectives will not be allowed to act arbitrarily on the construction of roads beyond the boundary without the permission and formal notification of the Public Security Bureau's jurisdiction. Mr. Everson expressed his regret and gave his verbal agreement, promising to respond formally in writing within two or three days. The Public Security Bureau has reported the incident to the Municipal Government. (China East News Agency)

Expressing Condolences to the Injured Policeman 207

Those who sent representatives to express their condolences included Ren Liping, Director of the Sixth District of the Public Security Bureau, and Liu Yunfang, Director of the Second Sub-Station of the Sixth District, who personally visited the hospital. In addition, Wang Zhijian and Jin Xihan from the Second Sub-Branch of the Ninth District of the Party Department, Zhu Shiqi and Lin Yanggao from the Sixth Sub-Branch of the Ninth District, Xie Qingbai and Lin Diangang from the Yanfu Association, Zhuang Yaoming from the Fahua District Farmers' Association, Zhou Chengxiang, Chairman of the Commercial Federation, Huang Smei from the Guard Corps, and more than twenty other people visited to express their condolences.

Serious Injuries 208

Kong Qingfeng was injured in the vital part of his right arm and was in great pain and mentally confused. When the representatives arrived at the hospital, the policeman endured the pain and spoke to the representatives with intermittent words, "Down with imperialism" and "Take back the roads beyond the boundary."

Concern for Road Rights 209

The Second Sub-Station of the Sixth District attaches great importance to this case. Director Liu has been determined to take back the road rights since he took office and has already drafted a plan and submitted it to his superiors. After the incident occurred, he worked even harder and submitted five more conditions to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for adoption yesterday.

Gathering of All Sectors 210

After expressing their condolences to the injured policeman, representatives from all sectors gathered in Xujiahui and planned to initiate the organization of a committee to automatically take back the roads beyond the boundary. They will not stop their efforts until their goal is achieved. They are currently drafting an outline and submitting it to their superiors, and will actively proceed after it is approved.

Declaration of the Party Department 211

The Second Sub-Branch of the Ninth District convened a temporary executive committee meeting yesterday to discuss countermeasures regarding the case of Western constables from Haig Road shooting policemen Kong Qingfeng and Yan Lunxing beyond the boundary without reason. It was decided that in addition to sending representatives to express their condolences to the injured policemen and issuing a declaration, Jin Xihan and Wang Zhijian were appointed to actively organize a committee to take back the road rights and request their superiors to commend Director Liu Yunfang for his effective handling and the injured policemen. Declaration (omitted).

The Railway Staff First Aid Training Class is Well Run 212

The Shanghai-Nanjing-Ningbo-Hangzhou Railway Administration, for the health and safety of employees and passengers, appointed its chief medical officer, Deng Zhende, to organize a first aid training class for railway staff. The chief medical officer selected medical officers to be in charge of training. The Guangxin Association Telegraphs Request for Swift Suppression of the Red Bandits in Eastern Jiangxi 213

The Guangxin Seven Counties Association sends a fast mail telegram to General Commander Jiang in Nanchang: Eastern Jiangxi is unfortunate. The Communist bandits Fang Zhimin, Shao Shiping, Wang Mingui, Zou Qi, etc., have wantonly ravaged it for five years. Countless people have been brutally killed and houses have been burned. The painful and tragic situation is unbearable to describe. This time, Your Excellency led hundreds of thousands of patriotic soldiers to Jiangxi to rescue the people from disaster. Upon hearing this news from the depths of our suffering, we could not help but rejoice and be moved to tears. Reports say that Your Excellency has arrived in Jiangxi Province and has a comprehensive plan to solve everything. The corner of eastern Jiangxi is adjacent to the three provinces of Fujian, Zhejiang, and Anhui, and its importance is self-evident. However, there is a limited garrison in eastern Jiangxi at present. The strength is weak. It is more than enough to defend, but there are concerns about taking care of one thing and losing sight of another in the suppression. Yesterday, refugees from Hekou said that the garrison in Hekou had captured many Red bandits in the last ten days, including Sun and Su. After interrogation, they confessed that after the bandit leader Fang Zhimin sneaked back to his old nest from Fujian, he planned to use force to go from Guige to Qian, Rao, Guang, and Yu, in order to connect with Zhejiang, Fujian, and Anhui. Currently, the seven counties are in great terror because of this. It is like a catastrophe is imminent and life is insecure. However, after checking the bandits' loose talk, it is not without effect, but the people who have suffered from the Red disaster for a long time are naturally like startled birds. In addition, seeing that the defending forces are not sufficient to cope, even the grass and trees on Mount Baigong seem like soldiers. Now, fortunately, Your Excellency, with a heart that regards the hunger and drowning of others as your own, braved the heat to come to Jiangxi to solve the suffering. At this critical moment, we earnestly request Your Excellency to grant our request, draw up elite troops as much as possible, and quickly open up eastern Jiangxi to avoid the long-suffering people from falling into the red terror again. If this area is not ground into powder, the Party and the country will be very fortunate, and eastern Jiangxi will be very fortunate. We cannot bear to wait impatiently. The Guangxin Seven Counties Association in Shanghai kowtows. Respectfully.

News on the Case of the National Products Department Store Yesterday 215

The Negotiation Committee Submitted a Request for Negotiation

Manufacturers and Employees All Decided to Petition

In the case of the National Products Department Store being ordered to close by the Public Concession, the Municipal Government has made a serious representation. Submitting a Request for Negotiation 216

The National Products Department Store Negotiation Committee submitted a document to the Central Party Department of the National Government, the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Industry, and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, stating, "This is a submission for a request. It has been found that the Chinese National Products United Department Store was illegally closed by the Public Concession's Public Works Department on June 9 of this year, and employees were beaten and arrested. The various acts of brutality have been respectfully reported to your departments, requesting a serious protest. Although the Shanghai Municipal Government's protest and the assistance of various organizations have repeatedly negotiated, there has been no progress. Who is without a heart and cannot be indignant? Therefore, in recent days, the excitement of the Shanghai citizens, the unanimity of the public sentiment, all have the determination to break the cauldrons and sink the boats, and the spirit of peaceful struggle. They will not give up until their goal is achieved. Manufacturers' Meeting 217

Chairman Liu Zhongying decided to send representatives to the Municipal Government, the Municipal Party Department, the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, the Industry and Commerce Visiting Bureau, and Yu Qiaqing, the Chinese Director of the Public Works Department, to request a serious protest to the Public Works Department as soon as possible to resolve the problem and avoid commercial difficulties.

Employees' Congress 218

All the employees of the National Products Department Store held a congress at 10:00 AM yesterday. It was decided: (1) To send representatives to petition Yu Qiaqing, the Chinese Director of the Public Works Department, to request his assistance. (2) To organize a propaganda team, appointing Cai Zhongliang as the general captain, Ye Hongxin as the captain of the first team, Yan Wenlian as the captain of the second team, Ye Zusheng as the captain of the third team, and Xi Tiegang as the captain of the fourth team, and Qiu Churong as the captain of the fifth team. (3) To report to the British government the process of the Public Works Department illegally closing the department store. (4) If the Public Works Department is not sincere in accepting the conditions, prepare for further resistance.

The YMCA Initiates an Inspection of Sanmen Bay 219

The Inspection Group is Scheduled to Travel

Sanmen Bay is located in the south of Xiangshan in Ningbo, Zhejiang, and north of Wenzhou. It is shaped like a gourd mouth and is extremely important. It is rich in products and convenient for transportation. It is a natural commercial port. The area has had an important history in ancient times. In recent decades, knowledgeable people in our country have repeatedly sought to revitalize it, but they have failed due to economic and human constraints. Recently, Xu Tingzuo, Wang Gechen, Fang Youdu, Xu Xinfu, etc., have raised funds to operate, and have registered with the National Government. Therefore, no less than thousands and hundreds of people have invested in the area. The docks and warehouses have been completed, and roads and various industries are also being built in order. The local YMCA believes that this move is a fundamental construction for the people's livelihood and can adjust both capital and talent. Therefore, it has decided to invite industrial experts from Shanghai and Hangzhou to hold a research meeting at the YMCA on Sichuan Road at 3:00 PM on the 29th and 30th of this month, and to continue to travel to Sanmen Bay from July 9 to 16 for field inspections. The YMCA welcomes anyone who is determined to revitalize industry, as well as experts in water conservancy, reclamation, animal husbandry, engineering, and manufacturing, and has printed brochures available upon request.

Butchers Throughout the City Went on Strike Yesterday 220

Most Stores Sold Leftover Meat Yesterday

If the Delay Continues, It Will Be Difficult to Meet Market Demand

The nine fresh pork shops in the city, including Changyuan, and all their employees, stopped business due to the butchers' failed attempt to force the purchase of fresh pork and the beating of employees. After the Bureau of Social Affairs sent personnel to persuade them, they resumed business that night. However, more than a thousand butchers throughout the city went on strike again yesterday. The various situations yesterday are recorded below.

Truth of the Beating 221

At 2:00 PM on the 23rd, when the Xuejia浜 fresh pork market was opening, a butcher named Zhang Xiaogen wanted to buy a pig from Changyuan pork shop and insisted on deducting three catties. Liang Anmin, an employee of the shop, agreed to deduct two catties. Later, another butcher bought it. Then another butcher, without asking the reason, punched Mr. Liang of the shop. Butcher Zhang was stabbed in the leg with scissors. The patrolman Kou Yuxi asked Shao Yunqing to take them to the First Sub-Station of the First District of the Public Security Bureau. After questioning by the director, because both sides requested to be transferred to the court, they were immediately transferred to the local court for processing.

Authorities Investigate 222

Because the pork shop employees were forced to buy fresh pork by the butchers, which led to the pork shop employees going on strike, the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs immediately sent staff member Gu Bingyuan to persuade them to resume work first and wait for the arrest of the perpetrators according to law. Unexpectedly, after the pork shop employees resumed work, the butchers went on strike again. Yesterday, Zhu Guilin was sent again to conduct a strict investigation to verify and handle the matter. In addition to sending police patrols, Xu Su, the director of the First Sub-Station of the First District of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, personally went to investigate the truth.

Pig Trade Resumes Operations 223

The nine fresh pig businesses in Xuejia浜, Changyuan, Shengyuan, Yuanda, Chunyuan, Yuhe, Changshun, Changhe, Rundda, etc., after butchers attempted to force the purchase of fresh pigs without success and gathered a crowd to beat up staff, insisted that the perpetrators be punished and refused to open for business. All the staff, because of the butchers' violent behavior, also dared not proceed with weighing the goods. All the fresh pig porters, in support of the staff, went on strike on the 24th, stopping the transport of goods. Fortunately, after the Society Bureau dispatched staff member Gu Bingyuan to mediate, the pig business staff and porters resumed operations and weighing and transporting goods at 6 PM that evening.

Butcher Strike 224

Butchers from Xinzha Road Su Xi Abattoir, Ninghai Abattoir, Yuezhou Road Juxing Abattoir, Zhabei Shenghe Abattoir, Xuejia浜 Chengxiang Abattoir, French Municipal Council Abattoir, Jiaxing Road Renyuan Abattoir, etc., went on strike yesterday morning due to a conflict between Zhang Xiaogen, a worker at Wanxing Abattoir, and partners of the Changyuan Pig Business, ceasing to transport pigs to the market and slaughter them. As a result, the usually bustling Xuejia浜 market is now unusually quiet.

Meat Market Panic 225

More than 20 fresh meat merchants in the Public Concession, French Concession, South Shanghai, and Zhabei, deeply concerned about not being able to procure goods due to the pig business shutdown the previous day, rushed to the market that evening upon hearing of the resumption of operations to purchase goods. Unexpectedly, the butchers suddenly announced a strike yesterday, so the goods purchased could not be transported to the abattoirs for slaughter. In this hot summer weather, overnight meat is not suitable for long storage. Most of the meat sold in the market today is already overnight meat. If the strike is prolonged, there may be no meat to sell tomorrow or the day after. Yesterday, a small number of fresh meat merchants went to Wusong to buy pigs in order to meet market demand. However, several businesses in the South Shanghai district had already run out of meat to sell and had to temporarily suspend operations.

Draft Penalty Rules for Business Tax in this City 226

The penalty rules for collecting business tax in Shanghai City have now been drafted by the preparatory office and are recorded as follows: Article 1: These rules are formulated in accordance with the provisions of Article 18 of the Shanghai City Business Tax Collection Regulations. Article 2: Those who violate the provisions of Article 11 and Article 17 of the Shanghai City Business Tax Collection Regulations and Article 3 of the Implementation Rules, and do not apply for a business license or fail to renew it when required, shall, in addition to being ordered to apply or renew separately, be penalized according to the following provisions: A. For the first offense, a fine of one to ten yuan shall be imposed. B. For a second offense, a fine of ten to twenty yuan shall be imposed. C. For more than two offenses, a fine of twenty to thirty yuan shall be imposed. Article 3: Those who violate the provisions of Article 11 and Article 12 of the Shanghai City Business Tax Regulations and underreport the amount of business capital or turnover shall, in addition to being ordered to pay the tax arrears, be penalized according to the following provisions: A. For the first offense, a fine of one to two times the tax payable shall be imposed. B. For a second offense, a fine of three to five times the tax payable shall be imposed. C. For more than two offenses, a fine of five to ten times the tax payable shall be imposed. Article 4: Those who violate the provisions of Article 11 and Article 12 of the Shanghai City Business Tax Regulations and conceal their income shall, in addition to being ordered to pay the tax arrears, be penalized according to the following provisions: A. For the first offense, a fine of one to five times the tax payable shall be imposed. B. For a second offense, a fine of five to ten times the tax payable shall be imposed. C. For more than two offenses, a fine of ten to fifteen times the tax payable shall be imposed. Article 5: Those who violate the provisions of Article 4 of the Implementation Rules of the Shanghai City Business Tax Collection Regulations and falsify account books or make false statements shall, in addition to being ordered to pay the tax arrears, be penalized according to the following provisions: A. For the first offense, a fine of five to ten times the tax payable shall be imposed. B. For a second offense, a fine of ten to fifteen times the tax payable shall be imposed. C. For more than two offenses, a fine of fifteen to twenty times the tax payable shall be imposed. Article 6: If a business operator fails to pay the monthly tax payable for more than one month, a late payment penalty of one-tenth shall be added. If the tax is not paid for more than two months, a late payment penalty of two-tenths shall be added. If the tax is not paid for more than three months, the business may be suspended, and the tax arrears and late payment penalty shall still be pursued. However, if the delay in payment is due to the delay in collection by the competent collection authority, no late payment penalty shall be added, and the penalty of suspension of business shall be waived. Article 7: Those who are subject to suspension of business due to late payment of business tax shall not be allowed to resume business until the tax and penalty are paid in full. Article 8: The fines imposed in accordance with these rules shall be notified by the competent collection authority to the penalized person for compliance and payment, and a fine receipt shall be issued when the fine is paid. The aforementioned fine receipt shall be issued by the Finance Bureau to the competent collection authority for use. Article 9: If the penalized person refuses to pay the fine, the competent collection authority may hand it over to the local Public Security Bureau district office for enforcement, or submit it to the Finance Bureau for verification. Article 10: Regardless of whether the fine imposed in accordance with these rules is discovered and punished by the personnel of the competent collection authority or reported by outsiders, 40% of the fine may be drawn for rewards, and the remaining 60% shall be reported and remitted along with the collection. Article 11: If there are any matters not covered in these rules, the Finance Bureau may revise them at any time and report them to the Municipal Government for record. Article 12: These rules shall be promulgated and implemented from the date of approval by the Municipal Government.

National Government Orders Investigation of Japanese Merchant Yarn Tax 227

Xie Rixin, representative of the Joint Federation of Japanese Factory Workers in Shanghai, submitted a petition stating that more than 100 Japanese yarn factories in Shanghai produce more than 300,000 bales of cotton yarn per month, and according to export tariffs, a tax of six cents is collected per bale, which could yield more than 180,000 taels per month, but it has never been collected. Is there another reason why national sovereignty is being lost? The National Government has handed this over to the Executive Yuan, which has forwarded it to the Ministry of Finance for investigation and verification.

Anti-Drug Conference Resolves to Oppose Prohibition in the Guise of Taxation 228

The Central Anti-Smoking Committee has established anti-smoking investigation offices in various provinces. The offices in various provinces have been announced one after another. From the observations of various parties, the establishment of anti-smoking offices in various provinces is to implement prohibition in the guise of taxation. Party departments and anti-drug groups in various places have declared their opposition and have filed petitions to the Central Government for correction. The China National Anti-Drug Association convened a meeting of its Standing Committee yesterday to discuss response methods and other important association affairs. The important resolutions are recorded as follows: (1) Regarding the adoption of prohibition in the guise of taxation by the Anti-Smoking Committee and the establishment of investigation offices in various provinces, after investigating its content, it not only violates the Hague Opium Convention and the KMT platform, but also greatly violates the Premier's anti-drug instructions. The association should adhere to the public opinion of the people and the party department, and continue to oppose it to maintain the prohibition of smoking. A large number of anti-drug instructions will also be prepared and distributed to various groups so that the public can understand the Premier's solemn proposition regarding the prohibition of smoking. (2) Approval of the Anti-Drug Propaganda Association Case: After reviewing the following eleven anti-drug propaganda associations, it was resolved that certificates should be issued to those who pass the examination to encourage them. As for those whose procedures are not complete, they will be urged to complete them in July so that they can be submitted for review and issued certificates. The list of qualified propaganda associations is as follows: Yancheng County Anti-Drug Propaganda Association, Jiangsu Province; Jiangyan Anti-Drug Propaganda Association, Taixian County, Jiangsu Province; Yangzhong County Anti-Drug Propaganda Association, Jiangsu Province; Zhenjiang County Anti-Drug Propaganda Association, Jiangsu Province; Rugao County Anti-Drug Propaganda Association, Jiangsu Province; Fengxian County Anti-Drug Propaganda Association, Jiangsu Province; Boli County Anti-Drug Propaganda Association, Jilin Province; Zhaoxian County Anti-Drug Propaganda Association, Hebei Province; Shenxian County Anti-Drug Propaganda Association, Hebei Province; Laiyang County Anti-Drug Propaganda Association, Shandong Province; Tonghe County Anti-Drug Propaganda Association, Heilongjiang Province. (3) The Anti-Drug Association in Singapore, Nanyang, sent a letter requesting the association to send personnel to assist in propaganda. It was resolved to appoint Chen Jun, professor of Zhejiang University and member of the Education Group of the association, to go. (4) Preparations for the 8th National Anti-Drug Movement Week this year: It was resolved that the daily names are as follows; detailed methods are to be determined by the secretariat: (1) Anti-Drug Instruction Day, October 1st (Thursday): Widely promote the anti-drug instructions of Premier and Lin Zexu, striving to thoroughly implement the spirit of the predecessors' prohibition of smoking and the Premier's anti-smoking propositions. (2) Anti-Drug Diplomacy Day, October 2nd (Friday): Awaken the public to commemorate the failure of our country's diplomacy due to the scourge of opium, and the current situation of national weakness and poverty, and jointly vow to strive to reject drugs, awaken attention to the obligations of the Hague Convention. (3) Anti-Drug Law-Abiding Day, October 3rd (Saturday): Make the people understand the laws and regulations prohibiting smoking, automatically abide by the law, and implement not planting, not manufacturing, not selling, not transporting, and not smoking, creating a strong and powerful public opinion to support the law, and urge the authorities to work hard to prohibit smoking according to the law. (4) Anti-Drug Petition Day, (Sunday): Hold a national anti-drug oath and petition, vowing to stand against opium and drugs and demanding that the government thoroughly prohibit smoking. (5) Anti-Drug Quit Smoking Day, October 5th (Monday): Pay attention to the anti-smoking movement, persuade addicts to quit smoking, and invite public and private hospitals across the country to rise up and promote the cause of quitting smoking. (6) Anti-Drug Family Day, October 6th (Tuesday): Publicize the tragic situation of family drug harm. To save the bad customs of society, we should pay attention to family anti-drug, so that it can fundamentally achieve results. (7) Anti-Drug Recruitment Day, October 7th (Wednesday): Widely recruit anti-drug comrades, increase anti-drug forces, promote the anti-drug monthly magazine, extensively promote anti-drug propaganda, and raise anti-drug donations.

Huiling Student Lan Jianye Commits Suicide Under Train 246

Unknown Reason

Suicide by Lying on the Rails

Lan Jianye, also known as Zhiren, a native of Dabu, Guangdong, was 20 years old. He transferred from the second grade of the Singapore Overseas Chinese Middle School to the Huiling English Training School in Xinlonghua, southwest of this city, last semester. He usually worked extremely hard, and his results in the summer final exam were excellent, ranking among the top students. Principal Qian Gengzhi allowed him to graduate. Now in school summer vacation. The students have all returned home, so since yesterday, meals have been stopped. However, a small number of students from other provinces, because there are no family members in Shanghai, still remain in the school. Lan is also a member of this group, so he still lives in dormitory 303. He got up at dawn yesterday morning, washed, and went to the exercise field to exercise. At about 8:00 AM, classmates and fellow villagers Qian Shaohua and Dai Miaofa invited Lan to eat noodles at the grocery store opposite the school, but Lan excused himself because of stomach pain and did not eat. He went north alone, walking straight to the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway. At that time, Lan was determined to commit suicide and had a firm will. He lay on the railway 200 steps northwest of the school, head north and feet south, using the rail as a temporary pillow, lying horizontally on it. Before long, a freight train from Hangzhou to Shanghai sped by and crushed him to death under the train wheels in an instant, his body and head separated. It is obvious that Lan was determined to commit suicide. The reporter, upon hearing the news, immediately drove to the scene of the incident to investigate. The body was wearing a white shirt, a white yarn sports vest, brown trousers, white socks, and yellow rubber sneakers. The head was inside the rail, and the body was thrown under the rail. Blue blood splattered on the muddy road, which was a terrible sight. He then went to the school and met with Principal Qian, who said that the student's father was dead and his mother was still alive. His brother Jianang works in a letter of credit company in Johor Bahru, Nanyang. The mother and brother are both in their hometown, and there are no relatives in Shanghai. When he came to school last autumn, Zhou Yede, a professor at Jinan University in Zhenru, was the guarantor for the student. He has now telegraphed to inform them. Before committing suicide, there was no sign of any abnormality, so the classmates did not suspect anything else. However, this spring, he had said to fellow villagers Shi Shuangchun and Guo Liuyu (students of Jinan University), "I must commit suicide in the future, and it would be most refreshing to die on the railway. After death, please bury me in the public cemetery in Jinan University in Zhenru (most of the young students from the South Seas who died in Shanghai are buried here)." Unfortunately, it has become a prophecy. Later, the local bailiff Zhang Guansheng reported it to the court for inspection. Prosecutor Yang was appointed to go to the countryside with the inspection official to inspect the body. He verified that Lan Jianye was crushed to death by a train before his death, so he filled in the corpse form and ordered the school to collect the body and temporarily place it.

Discovery of a Huge Quantity of Opium in a Passenger's Luggage 247

Li Qingzhen Goes to Claim the Seized Goods

Hoping to Make a Fortune

Yesterday, the Jinpu Railway Station Master telegraphed the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway Bureau, reporting that a passenger on Train No. 10 had multiple pieces of luggage containing a large quantity of opium and requested attention. Upon receiving the information, the Shanghai Bureau had the luggage thoroughly searched upon the train's arrival in Shanghai. Three large boxes of opium, weighing approximately 180 catties in total, were found in one piece of luggage. Shortly after, a man named Li Qingzhen arrived to claim the items and was detained and handed over to the Police Department. Under questioning, Li confessed that he was from Shandong and had partnered with three friends to purchase the opium in Luoyang. Hearing that Shanghai was about to levy taxes and that opium could be sold, they anticipated making a large profit and rashly engaged in this activity. However, they were misled about the prohibition of opium in Shanghai, resulting in a great loss. He pleaded for leniency. Given the large quantity of opium involved, both the person and the goods were transferred to the local court. After interrogation, Li was detained, and the drugs were confiscated, pending destruction.

Multiple Bandits Arrested

Officer Li led Police Chiefs Tian and Zhang, along with police officers from the Fourth District, Third Station, to investigate the aforementioned *bang bang* boats on the North City Shao River. Four people were found on board: Tao Guanghai, Tao Mao, Zhou Liangguo, and Tao Guanghai's son. During the search, Zhou Liangguo suddenly grabbed a bundle of clothes and fled ashore. After a chase, the police apprehended him. Inside the bundle were over ten pieces of clothing, sixteen pawn tickets, a ransom letter, and miscellaneous items. They were brought back to the team for interrogation. The confessions of Zhou and Tao were largely consistent. The main points were that they departed from Shanghai on April 12th with six people on board, led by Zhou Ermazi, and sailed to Baihe Port in Wujiang, where they robbed three families and kidnapped four people. They arrived in Dachang and were discovered by the militia on the fifth day of the month. They were taken, along with the stolen goods, to the Baoshan County Office. The previously stolen goods were divided into twenty-nine shares. The ransom letter was written by Zhou Haizi, Zhou Ermazi's son, who lived in Chedaijiao. Before the robberies, they had a meeting in a teahouse. There were two other accomplices, Dejun and Xue Renji, who lived behind the Dafeng Yarn Factory. Two Mauser pistols and a rifle were hidden under straw on the vacant coffin ground of the Chao Xi Bazijiao Bridge in Qibao. Officer Li inquired about previous robberies. Tao stated that on August 15th of the previous year, he had participated in a robbery outside the North Gate of Wuxi with Gao Gui and fifteen others, receiving eighty-seven yuan. After verifying the confessions, the officer dispatched police to a vacant lot in the 28th District of Qingpu, where they recovered a rifle and twenty-five bullets. Zhu Bailin, also known as Zhu Guoliang, an accomplice, was arrested in Xishi Shao, Jiangwan. His confession was similar. Yesterday, they received information that one of Zhou Ermazi's bandit boats was docked in Chedaijiao, and another was at Dayang Bridge. The police went to the locations. In Chedaijiao, they found a boat with three guards, Yang Chunshan, Huang Jinbiao, and Chen Zhenyu, who claimed to be detectives from Kunshan County and said that another boat had been sold by the detectives. Officer Li sent all the people, witnesses, and stolen goods to the main bureau for further investigation and legal action.

Two Maids of Judge Xiong Fei Disappear 249

One Is Now Found

Lured Away

The Seducer Is Sentenced

The Maid Is Sent to the Jiliang Institute

Xiong Fei, an execution judge of the Civil Division of the Special District Court, lived at No. 18 Rehe Road, near the Special Court. His two maids, Lai Fu and Lin Xi, were both nineteen years old and from Jiangxi, the same province as Judge Xiong. They suddenly disappeared simultaneously last month. Despite searching everywhere, they could not be found. As of the 14th of this month, there was still no clue. It was assumed that they had been abducted and hidden, possibly sold to other places. The case was reported to the Mixed Court, and the detectives were instructed to investigate thoroughly. Initially, there was no progress. However, the detectives of the Mixed Court received a tip-off from an informant that Lai Fu had been lured away by Shen, a Ningbo native and factory worker at the Laotongshun Cloth Factory at No. 204 Alabaster Road, and was cohabitating with him at No. 10 Wenjisi Road. The detective, along with a Western detective from No. 206, went to Shen's residence, arrested Shen, and found a pair of women's shoes but did not find Lai Fu. Upon questioning Shen, he confessed that she was at the Laotongshun Cloth Factory. They went to the factory, found Lai Fu, and brought them back to the court separately. However, the whereabouts of Lin Xi are still unknown. Yesterday morning, the detectives brought the man and woman to the Special District Court. Mrs. Deng, Judge Xiong's wife, was notified to attend the hearing. Judge Wu Tingqi opened the court. Wang Yaotang, the lawyer representing the police, stated that Shen Annan was being prosecuted for violating Article 257, Sections 1 and 2 of the Criminal Code for disrupting a family. He stated that Shen confessed to the police that he had seen Lai Fu for the first time in January of this year at a friend's house on Rehe Road, standing alone outside the door of her master's residence. He saw her again in February, but only glanced at her. On the night of the 27th of last month, he met Lai Fu on Kaifeng Road after returning from a show at the Xin Xin Stage. He asked why she was wandering alone late at night. Lai Fu said that Lin Xi had suddenly run away on the 25th, and she had gone out to look for her without success. She also said that she did not want to return. Shen, seeing that Lai Fu did not want to return, took her to Room 11 of a small inn on Chenjiabang, Avenue Edward VII, for two nights. They then moved to the Zhongnan Hotel on Baker Road for four nights. Finding the hotel expenses too high, he rented a house on Wenjisi Road and began to cohabitate. Since two women had disappeared at the same time, and Lin Xi had not yet been found, he requested that the case be adjourned. Mrs. Xiong then described the search for the missing maid. Lai Fu testified that she ran away because Mrs. Xiong treated her poorly and that her cohabitation with Shen was voluntary. She said that she did not know about Lin Xi's escape. Shen repeated his confession at the police station and insisted that Lai Fu's cohabitation with him was voluntary and that he did not lure her. Judge Wu ruled that the case had been investigated and was not related to Lin Xi's case and did not need to be adjourned. He immediately pronounced the judgment: Shen Annan was sentenced to six months imprisonment, reduced, for enticing a woman under twenty years of age to leave the person who had parental rights over her with the intention of immoral conduct. Lai Fu was ordered to be taken back by Xiong and Deng. However, Lai Fu, fearing further abuse, declared that she would never return to her former master. The police lawyer requested that the woman be sent to the Jiliang Institute for care. After deliberation, Judge Wu decided to send Lai Fu to the Women and Children Relief Association for temporary care.

Zoologist Mr. Kamp Brings a Turtle King from Southeast Asia 251

Mr. Kamp, an American naturalist, recently returned from an expedition to Southeast Asia, bringing with him many strangely shaped animals. The most unusual is a Turtle King, weighing about sixty pounds. Its head is like a python's. The back has thirteen large plates, each with peacock feather-like patterns. The tail is short, and the belly is white. The most noteworthy feature is that while ordinary turtles have claws on all four feet, this turtle's front two feet are like eagle's wings. It is very strong, roars like a tiger, breathes heavily, has hooked teeth, can bite people, and likes to eat fish. It is said that this turtle was stranded on a beach in Southeast Asia at low tide and was captured by Mr. Kamp. According to German zoologist Mr. Nall, if this turtle is allowed to grow its wings completely for two years, it will be able to fly. A gentleman from Wing On Company is now negotiating with Mr. Kamp to display the turtle at the amusement park for visitors to view and for zoologists to study.

Customs Seizes Foreign Ship Smuggling Taxed Goods 252

Over Ten Boxes of American Ginseng

Smuggled from Hong Kong

Since the implementation of the new tariff, ginseng and bird's nest tonics have been classified as luxury goods and are subject to extremely high taxes. Some merchants try to take advantage of loopholes and often evade customs duties. Yesterday, a British ship arrived in Shanghai from Hong Kong. When entering the port, the Jianghai Customs routinely sent officers on board to inspect the ship. They found a large quantity of American ginseng, over ten boxes, in the hold. There were also several packages of granulated sugar. Neither item was listed on the manifest, indicating an attempt to evade customs duties and port charges. It was pure smuggling, hoping to land the goods in Shanghai. After the customs discovered the goods, they considered that the value was extremely high and that, based on the new tariff, the tax evasion alone was significant. The shipping company would also lose considerable freight revenue. The goods were immediately seized and confiscated. There was no one to claim responsibility for smuggling the goods. The shipowner claimed to be unaware of the smuggling. The shipping company has questioned the crew responsible for the hold. The hold staff stated that they were unaware of the large amount of smuggled goods. The goods have now been stored in the customs warehouse. An investigation is underway to identify the tax evader and the person who smuggled the goods in order to impose a severe penalty.

Shanghai Ferry's Special Class Fare Increases Slightly 253

Effective Tomorrow

Since the City-operated Pujiang Ferry established special-class cabins, it has paid attention to all aspects of comfort, cleanliness, and aesthetics. Combined with the speed and convenience of navigation, people, both Chinese and foreigners, are happy to take the ferry to enjoy the river scenery and relax in the countryside. Recently, with the opening of the Gaoqiao route, the number of first-class passengers has increased significantly. The facilities of the special-class cabins must be further improved. However, given the rising cost of materials and high expenses, the Public Utilities Bureau has decided to increase the special-class fare slightly to increase revenue. The fare from Shanghai to Xidu will increase from 20 cents to 25 cents, Ning Temple and Donggou will increase from 30 cents to 35 cents, and Gaoqiao will increase from 42 cents to 50 cents. It is said that the new prices have been approved by the Municipal Government and will take effect on June 27th. The fares for the first and second-class cabins will remain the same, so there will be no impact on the burden of ordinary passengers.

Due to non-compliance with procedures, the Ministry of Communications of the National Government has ordered it to stop broadcasting. However, according to recent reports, the company is still broadcasting and has organized the China Broadcasting Association, distributing volunteer forms and soliciting members. This company is organized by foreign businessmen and dares to defy the orders of our Ministry of Communications. If it is allowed to operate freely without strict prohibition, the foundation of the country and the people will be greatly affected. Moreover, in Europe and the United States, foreign investment in radio stations is absolutely prohibited. The importance of this is obvious.
