Zhao Guanqing Sues Bei Runsheng Case 255

Continued Hearing and Debate Concluded Yesterday

Zhao Guanqing previously sued his uncle Bei Runsheng and cousins Zhao Zhulin and Zhao Pinhou in the Civil Division of the French Court for ignoring his advance payments. The hearing continued yesterday. The lawyer Lu Shaozong, representing the defendant Bei Runsheng, stated that the plaintiff had consistently failed to provide evidence to support his claims. He questioned why Bei Runsheng's name was not listed as a shareholder on the Yi Sheng document if he was a shareholder. Bei Runsheng was only in a supervisory position, indicating that he was not a shareholder. He stated that Runji was only to indicate the cooperation between Zhao Yuting and Bei Runsheng. The witness Yu Qiaqing had previously testified that Zhao Yuting was Zhao Runji. He also stated that there was no evidence that his client had given 50,000 yuan to the plaintiff through Zhou Weishi as a loan for Yi Sheng. This loan was actually requested by the plaintiff from the defendant through Zhou Weishi, and the plaintiff issued a note stating that it was a friendly loan. Later, the parties reconciled and never mentioned Yi Sheng. He presented the note for review. Moreover, the case was twenty-eight years old. Why was it not brought earlier? Even if there was evidence, it would be barred by the statute of limitations. As for the intervenors, their claims were dependent on the plaintiff's case. Since the plaintiff had failed to provide any evidence, the intervenors' claims could not stand. He requested that the case be dismissed and that the plaintiff bear the litigation costs. The lawyers Li Zuyu and Jiang Baoli, representing Zhao Zhulin, Zhao Pinhou, and their five brothers, stated that their clients were all sons of Zhao Yuting. Zhao Yuting was indeed a shareholder of Yi Sheng. He withdrew his shares because the plaintiff Zhao Guanqing managed the business poorly. Zhao Yuting paid over 90,000 yuan to cover the losses, and a withdrawal agreement was made. Zhao Yuting later gave the plaintiff another 50,000 yuan. In 1928, Zhulin and others paid another 25,000 yuan, with the plaintiff stating that there would be no further disputes. How could he now bring this case? There was no evidence to support the claim that the plaintiff had advanced over 400,000 yuan. He requested that the case be dismissed. The lawyer representing the plaintiff Zhao Guanqing stated that the defendant's response had no sufficient basis. The two characters Run Ji at the beginning when Yi Sheng was opened was intended to represent the collaboration of Zhao Yu Ting and Bei Runsheng, and that the 90,000+ on the exit share was never paid though it was written to have been paid on that day, as such it should be seen as invalid. He further stated that the Plaintiff had repeatedly approached the defendant to ask for it, and this can be used as proof. The lawyer He Xianzhang representing the intervenors, Zhao Jingqing and others, gave a detailed account of the situation. After a lengthy debate, Judge Gong announced the conclusion of the debate and adjourned the hearing for judgment.

The elderly woman Xing Zhu, 79 years old, from Tongzhou, residing on Rue Poinsett in the French Concession, was walking on Rue de la Cathédrale at 7 PM on the 24th when she was hit by a car driven by a Westerner named Hertel (transliteration), license number 10007. Special Item

Report of the Feetham Commission, Volume II (Continuation 9) 267

Abstract translation of the fourth and fifth compilations

Chapter Eight 268

The last part discusses the shortcomings of the current method of land registration, points them out, and raises the following questions: In any revised land regulations, is it necessary to stipulate a provision so that the Public Works Department authorities can independently establish a real estate office to gradually take over the real estate duties of the consular offices and register the land with perpetual lease deeds held by Chinese and foreign residents located in the public concession? This real estate office will first be allowed to register the land that has always held consular deeds and has been registered by the consular office. The report suggests that if this real estate office can be established, a provision should be made to determine the status of the registrar in complying with various court orders, which are related to the issue of ownership of registered land in the public concession. The report also suggests that this real estate office should be under the control of the same court as the Public Works Department itself. There is also a layer that can be stipulated, that is, the registrar of the Public Works Department's real estate office may request instructions from the court on issues of practice, and may be sued in the court as a civil servant. The difficulties involved, the author has not neglected, but the author believes that the issue of whether a new system of land registration can be planned and implemented should be carefully considered. This is not only for the benefit of the Chinese and foreign local interests in the public concession, but also for the general interests of the public concession as a commercial center. After extraterritoriality is finally abolished, the land registration system of the consular office cannot exist alone. According to the proposed method, the establishment of the Public Works Department registration system is a preparation strategy, sufficient to create a foundation for the new system. After the abolition of extraterritoriality, this strategy, if added with certain restrictions, may also be maintained.

Chapter Nine 269

Discusses the recommendations on the court, limited to two topics: (A) the organization and jurisdiction of the court, and the powers it exercises, that is, those currently granted to foreign consular courts; (B) further regulations on Chinese courts in the public concession. Regarding foreign consular courts, it is pointed out in the report that although the method of hearing all cases has proven the value of an independent court, its existing organization is not without its shortcomings. The consular court is organized by the foreign consular representatives stationed in Shanghai. Whether they can have the special qualifications to exercise judicial power is not guaranteed. Moreover, the organization of the court does not include Chinese assessors, which is especially inconsistent with the new developments of constitutionalism. Regarding the future organization of the court, it is suggested as follows: the court must have at least three assessors, one of whom is appointed by the Chinese government, and the remaining two should be judges of foreign extraterritorial courts exercising judicial power in Shanghai. The number of cases handled by the court may not occupy all the time of the assessors who make up the court. Therefore, the author suggests that these assessors should be requested to be concurrently held by existing foreign court judges instead of being specially appointed separately. The report then makes a further suggestion as follows: In addition to exercising the judicial power currently exercised by the foreign consular court, the newly established court should also have a kind of jurisdiction to hear and adjudicate cases raised by the Public Works Department of the public concession regarding the interpretation of any provisions of the land regulations or the interpretation or validity of municipal regulations, and please be determined by the court. Regarding the Chinese courts in the public concession, two suggestions are made: (A) Regarding jurisdiction, as left: All civil and criminal cases occurring in the public concession, if the defendant is under the jurisdiction of the court, then the court's ability to hear the case is obviously an appropriate method. If there is any ambiguity in the existing agreement on this point, it should be interpreted clearly. (B) Regarding the remuneration of assessors and the guarantee of tenure, it is suggested to stipulate a kind of regulation so that the assessors of each court can receive more considerable remuneration. There is a method that seems appropriate to discuss, even if the Public Works Department of the public concession subsidizes some court expenses, and makes a certain committee of the Public Works Department, or any organization representing the public concession, can express opinions on the appointment and removal of assessors. If this type of plan can be implemented, it is also possible to discuss methods so that assessors can have tenure security that is not currently available, and so that each assessor will not be damaged by any changes in the scope of their duties. According to any method proposed, the courts are still completely Chinese courts, but the special circumstances of the public concession, as well as the international interests involved in the exercise of jurisdiction by Chinese courts in the public concession, are therefore recognized.

Chapter Ten 270

The title is "International Partnership," which summarizes the general nature of the suggestions regarding the revision of the current organization law of the public concession: When the author analyzed the main provisions of the land regulations, he paid attention to the international nature of all the existing organization laws of the public concession. As early as 1866, when the existing land regulations were drafted, it was recognized that the "Chinese component" required by the municipal system was still lacking. It is obvious that the international nature of the organization law is still incomplete when this component is still lacking and the Chinese cannot participate in the three administrative, legislative, and judicial organs stipulated in the organization law. The first practical recognition of the Chinese in the public concession's request for this participation was the addition of Chinese directors to the board of directors. The author's current suggestion is that in addition to setting up Chinese directors, it should also be stipulated: (A) Holding a representative assembly of Chinese taxpayers, whose status is the same as that of the foreign taxpayer assembly; (B) Adding Chinese representatives to the agency that has the right to approve the regulations set by the Public Works Department; and (C) Adding Chinese representatives to the court controlled by the Public Works Department, and suggesting the establishment of various methods to expand and strengthen the existing partnership basis of various foreign countries regarding the affairs of the public concession. The development methods of such suggestions are all in accordance with the international partnership principle contained in the organization law. If these types of regulations are adopted and based on the willingness of the countries concerned to cooperate, and implemented fairly, it is hoped that the public concession system, which has a very extraordinary history in all aspects, will be able to fulfill its duties in a more complete and consistent manner in the future, and will be able to gradually adapt its methods and affairs to the needs of the new situation, while maintaining its outstanding characteristics that make it have special nature and value. Is it not reasonable? This is the result that the author has always had in mind when formulating various suggestions, and it is also the result of any reform suggestion. As for the complete success of this result, the extent of the benefits directly or indirectly involved has been pointed out and emphasized in the previous chapters. (End)

Free Talk

World Anecdotes 271

— Sea Guest

Rat Week

In recent years, our country has generally used seven days as a period for various public movements and added a new term "week," such as "Health Movement Week" and "Drug Prohibition Movement Week," and so on. In the winter of 1929, the whole of England also held a week. The name was very special and called "Rat Week." "Rat Week" was originally initiated by the Ministry of Agriculture and Fisheries of the British government and fought against millions of rats across the country. According to their survey, the number of rats is almost the same as their population. The consumption of each rat is one shilling per week. Then the total consumption per year is at least between 100 million pounds and 150 million pounds. The reason why they held this rat week is that it was just the time when the rats moved from the countryside to the towns. They had to come in groups like a human army. In advance, they sent scouts to see the situation. The local authorities planned to launch a large-scale attack after they were dispatched. The rats were about to suffer.

Smart Cat

In Catford, England, there is a black cat named "Tiger." It is very smart by nature. Every time it comes out to play from its owner's home, it can rotate the door handle with its two front feet and gently open the door. When it comes back, it stands on the door handle outside the door and stretches a foot up to knock on the door knocker. The servants come out to open the door for it. These actions are really the same as humans.

On International Debates 272

— Xu Wusheng

(1) On the tram giving up seats. A Westerner suddenly said to a Chinese friend, "Hey. You are too unreasonable. Just now I saw your country's modern woman on the tram. I stood up and gave up my seat to her. But later a Western woman came into the car and stood here. Why don't you give up your seat for her to sit? This is where you are wrong."

A Chinese friend replied, "Why should I give it to her? She has enjoyed this right in our China for decades. It doesn't matter if I let her stand for five minutes now. You should understand that women in the world treat men too unequally. Now our doctrine is to overthrow inequality. If an old, young, or weak man comes, I will still let him sit. This is the meaning of so-called supporting weak nations. If a young woman comes, I don't want her to give up her seat to me either. I just want to keep my own seat."

(2) Handgun Carrying Case A Nanyang overseas Chinese holding a first-class passport carried a large sum of money when landing in the Americas. The people in the US Customs saw a person with a first-class passport. They had to protect him specially, so they said to the landing overseas Chinese, "Are you carrying a handgun?" The overseas Chinese said, "I don't have a handgun." The customs officer said again, "If you don't have your own handgun, you are not allowed to land. Because it is very dangerous for the wealthy not to have their own handguns. Our police can't follow you around all the time." Later, the overseas Chinese bought a handgun before being allowed to land. This was what the overseas Chinese told a Chinese friend.

But a Chinese friend said to the overseas Chinese, "It shows that where you live abroad is very dangerous. You have to have your own handgun to live there. If you come to our real motherland to import and land, please throw away the handgun you bought abroad before you are allowed to land. Because our real motherland doesn't need handguns. It shows that it is much better than foreign countries."

(3) Insurance Claims Case An Indian businessman in Singapore built a summer house on a mountain in the city. There was no one nearby. One day, the house was burned down due to electrical failure. Fortunately, the house had fire insurance of 500 pounds of English gold, so he claimed compensation from the insurance company. Unexpectedly, the insurance company was a certain royal insurance company, which was very powerful and unwilling to pay compensation. Therefore, the Indian sued in court. On the day of the trial, the judge said to the Indian, "Your house is on a mountain in the air, a separate house. There is a suspicion of arson for compensation. According to the law, compensation cannot be paid."

An Indian asked the judge, "If a ship burns in the ocean, will compensation be paid?" The judge said, "A ship is a ship. A house is a house. There is a big difference." The Indian said, "There is no difference. The so-called difference is the difference between white and black. If the house is owned by a white person and the insurance company is owned by a black person, compensation must be paid."

(4) "Suitable for Death" and "Bleeding" Case An English aristocrat got lost in Tokyo. He saw a Chinese man in a suit and wanted to ask him the way. But when he saw the Chinese man, he looked like a Japanese and also like a Chinese. So he couldn't help but ask, "What Nese You Are?" meaning "Which kind of 'suitable for death' are you? Is it 'Chinese' or 'Japanese'?"

The Chinese friend in Tokyo was both amused and annoyed when he heard this question. He looked at the man carefully. He looked like an Englishman and also like an Irishman. He also asked him, "What Ish Aou Are?" "Which kind of 'bleeding' are you? Is it 'English' or 'Irish'?" The aristocrat got this kind of equal treatment and slipped away.

A 600-Year-Old Giant Tortoise 273

— Wei Cun

Recently, a Ryukyu islander caught a giant turtle six feet long near Naze Port in Okinawa Prefecture. The owner of the Osaka Kaiyukan aquarium bought it at a high price and raised it for tourists to visit. The giant turtle was shipped from Ryukyu to Japan on the Tainan Maru on the 15th of this month. It was unloaded at the Tomishima warehouse in Osaka. I happened to pass by there and saw the giant turtle raising its head and wailing sadly. Because it could not move due to the shackles, it shed tears like rain. I asked the guard about its origin. I learned that the turtle had a wine spleen. It cried every night during the voyage, causing the passengers to be unable to sleep. If given wine, it would stop crying. I didn't believe it, so I bought two bottles of wheat wine to try it. It drank it all in one gulp. The crying stopped. I asked Dr. Sato, the owner of the aquarium, about the age of the giant turtle. According to him, the turtle's development is only one pound per year, and the weight of the turtle is 563 pounds. It can prove that the age of the giant turtle is definitely over 600 years old.

The 22nd of this month was the 30th birthday of Zhao Junhao. Zhao Jun's friends specially held a celebration at the Dongya Restaurant. That night, there were more than 300 male and female guests. Unfortunately, Cheng had a foot disease and Jiang returned home. Xun had to perform the full version of Yutangchun that night. He had to go on stage at 8:30 PM, so he came to congratulate him at 7:00 PM and left in a hurry. That night, the musicians were Wang Ruoqi and Liu Bilin, two amateur erhu players from Shanghai. They were masters of the art, which caused a burst of applause and added a lot of color. The pure singing began at 8:00 PM. First, Ms. Shi Xiuwen sang two sections of the original Ban Xipi of Yu Bei Ting. Her voice was clear and her rhyme was mellow. Then, Ms. Min Cuiying sang the Detective Shaker of June Snow, which was also sad and moving. Ma Zhishan's Cui Ping Shan, Wu Qianan's Zhan Taiping, Zhu Liwen's Fen He Wan, Li Huapu's Kong Cheng Ji, and E Lu Gong's Wu Ben Ji were either good at singing in a high voice or good at speaking. There were too many beautiful things to mention. Yan Jupeng sang a section of the original Ban of Hongyangdong. The ups and downs were indeed extraordinary. As soon as one section was finished, there was an endless stream of voices asking for another one. As a result, he sang a few more verses of the shaker before stopping. Madam Chen Yihong's Kunqu opera Asking for Illness had an elegant charm. Yu Kongwo's Famen Temple was a section of Xipi slow Ban turning to 261. The singing was calm and well-organized. Ms. Ma Shufen's Ma Dian, a large section of Erhuang, did not slack off until the end. It showed that she had a deep foundation. Finally, Zhou Jianyun, Ms. Hu Die, and Ms. Liang Saizhen sang the Siping Tune of Mei Long Zhen together. The singing was melodious and pleasing to the ear. It was followed by Qian Ruifu's Yu Cang Jian. He learned Uncle Yan's singing method very vividly, which was not easy. It was not until 11:00 PM that everyone dispersed in joy.

Indian Travel Notes (52) 275

— Ling Hua

15th Recently, a conflict between Muslims and Hindus occurred in Varanasi. They fought for several days. Sixty or seventy people died and two hundred were injured. The reason was that foreign goods were checked. Indians boycotted British goods and were not allowed to sell them. Some Muslims sold British goods and were killed. It was suspected to be Indians, which led to a major conflict. Varanasi is a very peaceful holy place. It is strange that this phenomenon occurred. It gives the British an excuse. There have always been conflicts between Indians and Muslims in various places. Only this place has none. It is strange and lamentable that so many people have died and been injured. It is also a major obstacle to Gandhi's movement. On this day, I gave a speech at the Muslim Students' Association. Each student room is one room. It is spacious and clean. In India, classes are held from 10:00 AM to 3:00 PM every day. The Muslim Students' Association also has a head teacher who leads the prayer report. From January 20th to February 20th, Muslims fast during the day for a month. Those who fast during the day can eat once before 4:00 AM every day, and twice after 5:00 PM until night. Indians thought it was strange. I asked my Muslim friend and said that fasting has several advantages. One is to get rid of diseases. The second is to know the situation of the poor. The third is that if you encounter an extremely dangerous situation, you can practice resistance. This is the meaning of fasting. I think his leader must have had more difficulties when he used troops in the beginning. Most of them ate at night and fought during the day, so they became accustomed to it and made it a permanent commemoration. Night eating and day fighting are most suitable for using troops. Alas. Life is the most difficult. I told my Muslim friend that there are only three roads for each leader. One is to be killed, like Jesus on the cross. The second is to kill, like Muhammad. The third is to run away, like Buddha and Lao Tzu. There is no good way up. Killing and being killed are both last resorts.

16th The Englishman Florenk Garding and his wife invited me to dinner. I met Sura Ni, who had traveled to China. Garding introduced me to several beauties. I went to Simm's American rural beauty place with them. I passed a long iron bridge, which was about half a mile long. The cost of this bridge was very large. The bridge is divided into three lanes, with upper and lower floors. Trains, large vehicles, and human vehicles can pass through without hindrance. This river is the Ganges. The water of the Ganges is clear here, not as turbid as in Jia City. Every time I think of the Ganges, I always remember the story of King Bosi's mother in the Surangama Sutra. I got a poem as follows. I used to read the Surangama Sutra. Now I see the water of the Ganges. There was a great enlightened fairy. I used this to prove the wonderful meaning. The bright moon shines in the sky. Thousands of rivers are like mirrors. The water flows and the moon shadows move. The moon today is not the same as the past. Water and moon are like change and destruction. Not to mention the skin and bones. I only think of my kind mother's grace. I will never forget it. Mother transforms away the killing intention. The repayment of kindness starts from now.

Novelists' Rotary Club

??? (3) 276

— Xu Zhuodai

Ziliang had no way to deal with this innocent and naive wife. As a school teacher, he had worked hard for six days in the classroom. Today was Sunday, and he should have rested and slept in a little later. Who knew she would come and disrupt his sleep? Could he say she was ignorant? She had, after all, graduated from junior high school. However, she was inherently mischievous. Ziliang felt ashamed that he, an educator, couldn't influence his closest companion.

"Didn't you say a few days ago that you would take me out to play on Sunday?"

"Take you out to play? Where to?"

Ziliang couldn't remember for a moment.

"You said you'd take me to learn swimming, to the Hongkou swimming pool!"

He thought, he did say something like that; but now that he remembered, today wouldn't work. In just five or six days, summer vacation would begin, and he had three classes' worth of compositions, totaling over one hundred and sixty, that he needed to finish grading today. Delaying any longer would be too late. Thinking of this, Ziliang didn't feel like sleeping anymore. Grading over one hundred and sixty compositions in a single day might be impossible, so he might as well get out of bed early. He made up his mind and jumped out of bed. His wife, seeing this, also got up.

"That's right! As soon as you hear about taking me swimming, you're willing to get up! That's a great black lacquer stool!"

"No! I don't have time today. I have to grade papers."

"If you don't take me, I'll ask another man to take me! Then you'll be fighting to go with me!"

Ziliang didn't even hear what his wife said. He got dressed and went downstairs. Yueru also hurried downstairs. The nanny in the kitchen, seeing the master and mistress come down together, was glad she had prepared the washing water early. She brought out a basin of washing water and placed it on the table. Ziliang went over to wash his face, but his wife pushed him aside:

"Husbands and wives should respect each other like honored guests. Why are you respecting me like a soldier, fighting to grab it? I got up first today, so this basin of washing water is mine!"

Seeing her go to wash her face, Ziliang went to rinse his mouth. When the second basin of water was brought, he washed his face.

For auxiliary coin trading, the Jiangjiao was 3,500 jiao in the early market and 2,000 jiao at noon. The Guangjiao was 100,500 jiao in the early market and 65,000 jiao at noon. There were over 33,000 strings of copper coins.

Securities and Public Bonds for June Term Will Be Suspended Today 287

Yesterday, the 20 Customs Bond Rose Significantly, and Others Were Also Slightly Firm

The Provision of Physical Goods for July Term Futures Has Been Cancelled Yesterday

Yesterday was the last day of trading for public bonds with a June term. It will be suspended today in preparation for delivery. The exchange has cancelled the restriction on the provision of physical goods for futures trading in the July term. However, for the new August term futures trading opening tomorrow, the sale is still limited to the provision of physical goods. Checking yesterday's public bond market conditions, the spot market was still weak, and the futures market was still active. The market atmosphere was lively, and the initial trend in the morning was weaker, with more declines than the previous day. The second session then turned uniformly firm, and there was little change in the two sessions of the after-market, because the market supply and demand situation was balanced. As a result, there were more rebounds than before. Only the 20 Customs Bond rose significantly, with the June term rising by 1 yuan and 7 jiao, and the July term also rising by 1 yuan and 3 jiao. Other bonds rose by about half a yuan. It is estimated that only 10,000 yuan was traded in spot goods throughout the day, and the total futures trading was over 24.8 million yuan. Among them, the trading volume of the July term increased much more than before.

Yarn, Cotton Yarn Market Downturn is Severe 288

The yarn market has fallen sharply, and the situation is very weak. The fluctuating gold price has caused people to be flustered, so the market is very soft. The sales of existing yarn are relatively sluggish, but export transactions to the East are continuous. However, the selling pressure is very fierce, so the thoughts of scattered investors are becoming more and more weak, and they can only bear the pain to close their positions. Therefore, the market is trending downstream. However, the bottom goods of various factories are reduced compared to before. In short, the exchange rate news is not good, so the short side is very focused and it is not easy to rise sharply for the time being. However, most bulls are still unwilling to let go, it is said.

The Human Standard Uniformly Decreased by 2 Taels and 45 Qian 289

At the opening of the human standard pre-market, the American cotton was flat, and the gold price fell, causing people to panic again. The prices for each month fell by 1 liang, 6, 7, and 8 qian. In the afternoon, the bidding for yarn was still unfavorable and fell by another 5, 6, and 8 qian. The total transaction was estimated to be 48,050 packages. It was found that Heshen sold 1,350 packages, Jifeng 1,300 packages, Tianlong 1,400 packages, Shenji 1,600 packages, and Deji 2,550 packages. Tongyu bought 1,200 packages, Gengfeng 1,600 packages, Yongfeng 1,150 packages, Yichang 1,650 packages, and Yiyu 1,650 packages. The closing price is recorded on the left.

Foreign Cotton and Yarn Slightly Rebound

American Cotton Rebounded Ten Pounds 294

Yesterday, American cotton was initially weak due to pressure from sellers, but later became firm due to the strength of Wall Street and purchases by the public. Silk and Tea Factories' Sales to France Still Not Desolate 296

New York Prices Reported Higher... Factory Purchases Still Watching and Waiting

Yesterday, the Japanese and British firms' silk market still lacked the possibility of progress. Although New York silk prices were reported higher, factory purchases were watching and waiting. However, sales to France were not desolate. Lyon continued to send telegrams for transfers. Yesterday, Dachang and others imported 40 packages of Shanghai White Raw Silk, and Xinfu imported 20 packages of Sichuan Yellow Raw Silk. Prices were said to be firm.

Needle and Eyebrow Green Tea Sales to Europe Smooth 297

Yesterday, the needle and eyebrow green tea from inland firms was sought after by British firms such as Jardine Matheson, Ewo, Concord, Jinlong, and Fushi. Transactions were still not desolate, and selling prices were quite firm. The bud-picked Zhenmei was slightly favored by Dodd, Forbes and others, with top prices quoted at 270 taels. The market for ordinary Zhenmei remained sluggish. High-quality goods from Wuyuan's northern route firms were not quoted on the market yesterday. There were no large transactions for other goods such as Gongxi and Xiumei.

Grain and Rice Market Gradually Loosening

New Wharf 298

Yesterday, the rice market saw a lack of early morning bids for Changshu and Xianzi rice. By the afternoon, the strength reached numbers 32 and 33. However, the City God Temple and Xiutang Rice Industry Association are in the period of comparing measures, with a total of 240 boats compared, so transactions on this street were extremely quiet. Only about 1,000 piculs were sold in small lots. The opening prices for especially top-quality rice fluctuated by a few cents, while medium-quality rice shortened by about two dimes. There was no activity in the thin rice measures from Shipu, Chonggu, and Xitang, with the situation softening by two or three feet. Although Yangdu superior rice was in short supply, local shops were unwilling to purchase more, and the price fell by nearly a foot. The supply of superior rice from Babu was still thin, and the price was short by half a foot. Glutinous rice was dull, and distillers' appetite was meager, indicating a sluggish downstream.

South Shanghai 299

Yesterday, although the supply from various regions was thin, the amount in Puxun gradually thickened. Due to the extremely hot weather and news of cheaper prices in the northern market, both urban and rural shops were watching and waiting. Moreover, the appetite of the firms was also thin, and coupled with the difficulty in storing goods for long, they had to loosen their prices accordingly. The sales volume was also not selective, resulting in a repeated decline in the price of thick japonica rice, shortening by about two dimes. The supply of thin indica rice seemed scarce, but those with accumulated stocks were slightly loosening, due to the continued arrival of Songjiang rice, resulting in no demand from Ningbo. Although there was some activity in this street, it was only in small lots, and the market price shortened again by two or three dimes. Sales of Luyang superior rice and arrivals were balanced, with no gains or losses. The glutinous rice market was still active, with dozens of piculs traded at prices unchanged.

Flour and Wheat Also Affected by Gold Prices

Wheat Flour 300

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning and afternoon, the prices for all months uniformly showed a sharp decline. Although the quoted prices for foreign wheat were better by about two, three, or four dimes, domestic and international environments had shifted their focus of observation since the sharp change in gold prices. If the exchange rate increases, foreign wheat can be readily fixed. At a time when new wheat is being harvested domestically, this impact is naturally more significant. Moreover, the factories' bargaining chips have been allowed to float recently, with no intention of buying them back. For the more distant months, they have been actively unloading for days, causing great shock and a rush to follow the trend, making the market atmosphere unsalvageable. Judging from the subsequent trend of actual sales not supporting purchases, it will be difficult for this month to pass steadily. Transactions were still smooth throughout the day, reaching over 170 bags. As a final result, this month fell by 2.75 fen compared to the previous day, July fell by 1.75 fen, August fell by 2.75 fen, September fell by 3.25 fen, October fell by 3 fen, and November fell by 3.75 fen.

Wheat 301

Yesterday, after the opening of the wheat futures market in the morning and afternoon, the prices for all months uniformly showed a sharp decline. With the fall in gold prices and the sharp rise in exchange rates, inquiries from abroad were very active. Domestically, supplies were flooding in from all over the place, while factories seemed to be feigning ignorance. By this point, the minds of those inside and outside the industry were inevitably apprehensive. The huge impact yesterday was due to the fact that the foreign wheat test orders placed by firms a few days ago were now confirmed due to the extended exchange rate. It was heard that traders had collectively ordered a ship of Australian wheat, to be shipped in August, at a combined price of 4 taels and 2 mace. It was also heard that factories had transacted for three ships, but the prices were not yet known. As a result, there was a surge in unloading, and many new bargaining chips were released, causing the market atmosphere to plummet. This month, with settlement approaching, those outside the industry were eagerly closing their positions, further exacerbating the decline. As a result, this month fell by 1 mace and 2 fen compared to the previous day, July fell by 6 fen, August fell by 8 fen, September fell by 7 fen, October fell by 8 fen, and November fell by 6 fen. Regarding the spot wheat situation, due to sluggish factory purchases and unusually weak sentiment, the price of medium-quality wheat was shouted down by about 2 mace yesterday due to standard issues. Over 1,000 bags of Nanjing, Chuzhou, Yangzhou, Penglai, and Anting wheat were opened, reportedly purchased by Fuxin.

Piece Goods Gradually Declining 302

The piece goods market was even more sluggish yesterday. With the continued decline in the gold market and the lack of vitality in yarn and cotton, people were fearful, and those holding goods were seeking to sell them off. Even the out-of-town dealers reversed from buying to selling, resulting in very quiet actual sales. Both local and out-of-town dealers were watching and waiting, and transactions were scarce. Yesterday, straight tribute broadcloth all fell in price, with Liyan Muqiu and Moganshan entering customs at 3 mace and 8 fen each. The Four Gentlemen had returned to 3 mace and 2.5 fen. Yuehua Silver had successively arrived in Shanghai, resulting in an oversupply situation. Prices fell by about 5 li compared to before. Foreign yarn was even more sluggish, with Dian Qiuxiang falling to 10 taels and 2 mace, Double Child Deer at 9 taels and 7 mace, and the price of upper body goods also softened. Little Beauty Li Taibai all fell. The stock of white crepe fabric increased again, with Tongpan returning to 4 taels 1 mace and 7.5 fen, and Human Dog at 4 taels 1 mace and 5 fen. Only bleached cloth still rose, likely due to low inventories and the arrival of the season. Yesterday, Dingfujun was sold at 12 taels, Magpie Bridge Meeting at 12 taels and 5.5 fen, and Blessing, Longevity, and Three Stars at 11 taels and 2.5 fen. Both colored strip velvet and mohair velvet had arrived in Shanghai, but the trend was quite quiet. The decline in western goods and foreign yarn was also severe. Huaji Butterfly Corridor and Teach Child brands fell by as much as 1 tael and 5 mace per piece compared to before.

Hardware from Shantou Dealers Suddenly Booming 303

Hardware transactions showed no progress yesterday. Factories and out-of-town dealers did not increase bulk purchases, resulting in a rather cold market. However, the Shantou dealers suddenly emerged and their business boomed, with transactions reaching over 1,400 piculs. The purchases consisted mostly of tinplate. It was also heard that there were quite a few French West nails, new lead wire, English steel plates, and angle iron. The market price remained relatively stable due to positive sentiment.

Hardware Merchants Temporarily Suspend Orders 304

Due to the continuous surge in foreign exchange rates, those who had previously settled import hardware goods at lower exchange rates suffered significant losses. Therefore, in order to maintain future market conditions, various firms in the market have temporarily suspended orders. It is said that foreign firms have had no new orders since yesterday.

North and South Goods: Dried Longan Prices Discussed for Increase Again 305

Due to the arrival of the moldy season, the inventory of dried longan at various firms has mostly been baked. However, baking inevitably increases costs due to weight loss, labor, and other factors. Selling at the current market price would certainly result in losses. Therefore, the trade association convened a meeting yesterday to discuss increasing prices in order to maintain costs. The proposed prices are: Top grade 36 taels, Heavenly grade 26 taels, Tianhong grade 20 taels, and Purchase grade 14 taels.

Book and Periodical Introductions

Northwestern Series 324

— Man Yin

By Lin Jing

Whether it be to consolidate national defense and prevent the invasions of various imperialist powers like Japan, Russia, and England, or to solve the problems of numerous unemployed and increasingly impoverished people in the interior, immigration to develop the border regions is a matter of utmost urgency at present. Can we stand idly by and watch Japan's occupation of the three northeastern provinces, Russia's redification of Outer Mongolia, and England's instigation of rebellion in Tibet, without thinking of ways to resist them? Can we stand by and watch the disasters of war and banditry in the interior, the daily worsening of people's livelihoods, and leave the excellent border regions, such as the forests of Jilin, the gold mines of Altai, the animal husbandry of Outer Mongolia, and the oil of Xinjiang, to be exploited by others without concern? As long as we are human beings, as long as our blood is still boiling and our breath is still coming and going, we, the youth who cannot find a way out in the interior, the unemployed masses, should go to the border regions in large-scale, organized groups. At the same time, our government should assume full responsibility for protection and safely transport our immigrant groups there. We must recognize that this is the only way to alleviate our difficulties, the only real way out for us.

The above paragraph is from a letter written to me by a friend who has already gone to the Northwest to investigate. I believe his words are correct, and I believe even more that his spirit of courage and perseverance will surely lead to success. Because I believe he is right, and because I admire and respect him, I have also developed the ambition to follow in his footsteps. Therefore, in recent times, I have felt a particular interest in matters concerning China's border regions, and I have been especially eager to collect works about the border regions, whether by borrowing or buying, even though money is so hard to come by.

After collecting hundreds of books about our country's border regions, I couldn't help but feel a nameless sorrow that pained my heart. It was that among these books, those that were more detailed and accurate were mostly translated from foreign languages. For example, an Englishman named Charles has written three thick volumes on the topography, roads, customs, human feelings, social system, politics, and economy of Tibet. Furthermore, Japan's works on Manchuria and Mongolia are beyond the reach of our Chinese compatriots. We cannot properly protect our own property, and we allow others to plot against us. Those being plotted against are still in a daze, like fish in a cauldron, leisurely and carefree, unaware of the impending disaster. What could be more lamentable in the world than this?

However, recently, this fact of our compatriots' neglect of the border regions, which caused me grief, has diminished a little. We cannot but thank Mr. Lin Jing for the publication of this Northwestern Series.

Mr. Lin is a traveler, and it can be said that he is one of the earliest Chinese people to pay attention to the problem of the northwestern border regions with scientific methods and political insight. I know from friends that he is doing what he believes he must do with an attitude of "taking what others discard." For example, in terms of immigration to the area and the development of the Northwest, which is now a fashionable tune sung to the high heavens, Mr. Lin already noticed it fifteen years ago and has traveled throughout the Northwest. Can we not say that he is a pioneer in the development of the Northwest?

"It possesses 2.38 million square miles, accounting for four-sevenths of the country's territory, containing the essence of the five elements and hundreds of products, being the starting point of historical culture, the source of rivers, the beginning of mountains, abundant for animal husbandry, vast for agriculture, controlling the hub of Eurasia, possessing natural raw materials, thus suitable for industry and commerce. As for the covetous eyes of strong neighbors, the hidden disputes of the world, the divisions of races and religions, and the security of the country, are these not the phenomena of the Northwest today? However, when presented to the people of the country, how many know of it? How many who know of it secretly ponder and plan to open up the wilderness, explore the treasure chest, and seek to create immortal achievements? Of those who do, how many can avoid making matters worse and turning blessings into misfortunes?... Alas, the beautiful rivers and mountains have turned into a field of Shura, and innocent people have become meat on the chopping block. Is this the inevitable result of fate, or is it that human affairs have not been exhausted?" (Preface to page one)

From this, we can know the author's ambition and interest in the Northwest issue. Because his vision is outstanding and he feels the importance of the Northwest issue to China and even the world, he does not hesitate to pursue and collect information in that border region, which is usually regarded as a world of ice and snow and a desolate landscape. This book is his record of the climate, topography, soil, customs, and human feelings along the way, "written from the ice and snow." From this, we can believe that it is an accurate record, unlike those who talk about the Northwest without ever having set foot there.

The entire book is divided into two parts, upper and lower. "(The upper part is a diary, divided into eight volumes. Volume 1: In the fifth year of the Republic of China, from Beijing via Henan, Shaanxi, Gansu to Dihua; Volume 2: In the sixth year of the Republic of China, from Dihua via the southern route of the Tianshan Mountains and Altai, Siberia to Beijing; Volume 3: From Beijing via Chahar, Suiyuan, Ningxia, Gansu to Dihua; Volume 4: From Dihua via Inner and Outer Mongolia to Beijing; Volume 5: In the fourteenth year of the Republic of China, from Beijing via Chahar, Suiyuan, Ningxia, Gansu to Qinghai; Volume 6: Record of residence in Qinghai from the fifteenth, sixteenth, and seventeenth years of the Republic of China; Volume 7: Record of circumnavigation of Qinghai in the sixteenth year of the Republic of China; Volume 8: From Qinghai to Shanghai in the seventeenth year of the Republic of China. The above eight volumes are compiled into six books, with the first, second, fifth, and sixth volumes each being one book, and the third and fourth volumes being combined into one book. The total number of words is about 800,000, and there are about 150 photos." (See Examples one)

Eight volumes, 800,000 words. This is a surprisingly large number. Regardless of its content, it is not something that can be written successfully in a short time just by putting black words on white paper. Only the third and fourth volumes combined into one book are published now. What is introduced below is these two volumes.

As mentioned above, the third volume records the journey from Beijing via Chahar, Suiyuan, Gansu, etc., to Dihua, and the fourth volume records the journey from Dihua via Inner and Outer Mongolia back to Beijing. The two volumes together contain about 200,000 words, which shows the richness of the material. They are all written in diary style. Although it feels a bit boring when reading, our focus is on the situation of developing the Northwest, investigation, and inspection of the Northwest, and not like reading literary works, requiring beauty and novelty in words and sentences.

Here, for the convenience of introduction, we can divide each volume into several parts to discuss.

Third volume: (A) From Beijing to Baotou, it took from November 13th to December 11th of the seventh year of the Republic of China. In addition to taking the train from Beijing to Fengzhen, 808 li, from Fengzhen to Baotou, it passed through Tiancheng Village, Haoqi, Shirenwan, Bikeqi Town, Taosihao, Salongqi County, a total of 670 li. From Beijing to here is 1478 li. (B) From Baotou to Ningxia, it took from December 12th to January 6th of the following year, passing through Hala Budha, Gagalqi, Jiangbai Store, Patu, Bulong Longxingchang, Xiong Wan's store, He Jia's village, Chinese Hall, Guangqingyuan, Changjia, Dengkou, Heguazi, Erzidi, Shizuizi Pingluo County, a total of 1208 li. (C) From Ningxia to Lanzhou, it took from January 7th to 21st, passing through Yanghe Fort, Daba, Qu Kouba, Shikong, Zhongwei, Shatouba, Changliushui, Gantangzi, Yingpanshui, Yitiaoshan, Dalabai, Liudun, Shuifuohe, a total of 905 li. (D) From Lanzhou to Suzhou, it took from February 8th to March 19th, passing through Zhujiajing, Xian Shuihe, Pingfan County, Gongkouyi, Long Goubao, Shuangdabaobao, Liangzhou, Forty Li Shop, Yongchang County, Shuiquanyi, Xinhebao, Dongle County, Zhangye County, Shahebao, Gaotai County, Huaqiangbao, Chiyanbao, Linshuiyi, Jiuquan County, a total of 1468 li. (E) From Suzhou to Hami, it took from February 20th to April 14th, passing through Jiaguguan, Huihuibao, Chijinxia, Yumen County, Sandao Gou, Bulong Jier, Xiaowanyi, Anxi County, Baidunzi, Hongliuyuan, Daquan, Malianjing, Xingxingxia, Shaquanyi, Kushuiyi, Geziyandun, Changliushui, Huanglu Wang, a total of 1362 li. (F) From Hami to Dihua, it took from April 15th to May 22nd, passing through Toubao, Sanbao, Sandao Ridge, Liaodun, Yiwanquan, Qigeying, Toushui, Dashitou, Sangequan, Muleihe, Qitai, Fuyuan County, Santai, Fukang County, Gu Mudi, a total of 1420 li. In total, it took about half a year from Beijing to Dihua (including time spent on the way), a total of 7842 li.

Fourth volume: (1) From Qitai, Xinjiang, to Lower Mongolia.

Page 22

Baidunzi, it took from June 7th to 17th, passing through Dongcheng Canal, Hongliu well, Jiji Lake, Black Mountain Head, Guai Ba Water, Guodi Mountain, Zhuanjin, a total of 730 li. (2) From Lower Baidunzi to Zhamushandan, it took from June 18th to 27th, passing through Five Households, Zhenxi County, D窖 Pu, Luanshanzi, Laoye Temple, Liuquan, Hengshanzi, a total of 700 li. (3) From Zhamushandan to Suo Temple, it took from June 27th to July 8th, passing through Hala Die Ling, Jia Hui, Jia Lameng, Suo Moda, Da Tuo Lei, a total of 725 li. (4) From Suo Hongtu to Jiaer Han Longtou, it took from July 9th to 18th, passing through Hei Sha Tu, Hao burst, Hala Niu Dun, Xue Hai, a total of 625 li. (5) From Jiaer Han Longtou to Zhang Mao Hala Tuoluo Gai, it took from July 19th to 30th, passing through Shan Dan, Ding Gai Hutong, Dara Wusu, Xiao Kui Teng, Xi Ba, Nao Hai Tu, a total of 668 li. (6) From Zhang Mao to Guihua, it took from July 30th to August 15th, passing through Yike Bula, Jian Ye He Sha, Xila Hada, Wula Bula, Ha Sha Tu Xi, La Mao Zhaoli, a total of 996 li, a total of 4440 li, taking about two months.

From the statistics of the number of places traveled in these actual locations, relying on the 18th-century transportation equipment in the north, the author of the book was able to travel all over the important roads in the Northwest. Can we not admire his endurance and enterprising spirit? After reading this book, what should we lament about our usual neglect of the Northwest, and what attention should we pay to it now? In terms of length, the third volume is longer than the fourth volume. This is because the area from Beiping via Chahar, Suiyuan, Ning, Gansu to Xinjiang is more important than the area from Xinjiang via Mongolia to Guihua. The former road almost passes through a very fertile area. Everything about customs, human feelings, politics, and economy is worth our attention and discussion, which the latter, mostly some Gobi deserts and uninhabited places, cannot compare to. Therefore, the author narrates more, giving us a clear and concise understanding of everything about the Northwest, such as roads, climate, topography, and other people's customs, habits, historical sites, etc. We think it is very clear and concise.

Secondly, there is also detailed investigation and narration on the resources of the Northwest. I cannot quote much from the original text here, but only briefly mention a few points scattered in the book.

(1) From Fengzhen via Wuyuan Baotou to Xinjiang, there are coal mines almost everywhere along the way.

(2) Jin is most famous in areas such as Suzhou and Ganzhou in Gansu.

(3) Carpets from Salachi County in Gansu, forests from Gucheng in Xinjiang, and animal husbandry from other places.

(4) Agricultural products from Liangzhou, Suzhou, Wuyuan, etc., such as beans, wheat, cotton...

In short, the fertile land considered in the interior is not lacking in the Northwest, and because the population is sparse, the land price is cheap, which is hundreds of times lower than that in the interior. We who have not been to the Northwest always think of the Northwest as a desolate border region. Now, after reading the narration in this book, can we not be moved?

At the end of the book, there are also many important papers such as the Survey of the Gansu-Xinjiang Road Opinions, the Northwest National Road Route Accounting Book, and the Survey of the Baotou Near Water Transport Situation Opinions, which help us to have a more clear and concise understanding of the work, preparation, and effort that should be made in the development of the Northwest. Before there are more detailed works that discuss and investigate the Northwest, I think this book is the only detailed book about the Northwest.

Finally, the reporter personally sincerely pays tribute to the author of this book and Mr. Zhao who sent the book for review, for allowing me to have a more detailed understanding of the Northwest before I went to the Northwest.

Casual Notes on Youth 325

— Yi Hua

Published by the United Bookstore

School life is a beautiful dream. This dream gives you many sweet and deep loves. If you have never entered the threshold of school, maybe you only have some empty dreams, but the actual inside story is ten times what you dreamed of. Especially the life of college students, college is a mysterious palace, all kinds of unimaginable interesting stories are being created, and beautiful stories are being played out. College students are natural darlings. They enjoy that beautiful dream with the era of youth. They are either the owners of those stories or the protagonists of those funny dramas, or at least a theater-goer watching the play. Many beautiful and interesting traces are deeply imprinted in their minds, and they often call out to cherish their unique youth.

The author of this book is a happy person who was once intoxicated in this dream. I read his works a long time ago and knew that he was a happy person who occupied the life of college students.

He is an author who is good at poetry and novels. Last autumn, I read his poetry collection "Fragrant Kiss," and this spring I read his collection of creations "Three Couples of Lovers," and recently I read this collection of essays "Casual Notes on Youth." Every time I read his works, I always feel a casual and humorous interest overflowing.

The author's poems and novels are of course what I love to read, but I think his specialty is especially writing essays. His essays have his unique beautiful and fragrant style. The material is the most beautiful part of life, and the style is the intoxicating spirit and lightness. Such essays are very worthy of attention and recitation among essays. Each section of "Casual Notes on Youth" is this kind of short note full of humor, tenderness, and suggestion. It is really a very good collection of essays.

The whole book is divided into three parts. The first part is "Casual Notes on the Light Moon," including twenty sections such as "Condensing Is the Jade Beauty Coming." The middle part is "Casual Notes on the Tender Breeze," including fifteen sections such as "The Girl Left Behind." The last part is "Casual Notes on the Fine Rain," including ten sections such as "Marriage Proposal Letter." Most of what is described here is the tender and beautiful school life, about men, women, teachers, and students. "For example, 'The Moon Is Especially Bright in Mid-Autumn' writes about life outside the school, while 'A Song of Manjianghong' describes the rhyme inside the classroom. 'The Girl Left Behind' writes about excessively beautiful girls, and 'The True Story of Ah Zheng' gives you a completely different taste. 'Affectionate But Annoyed by Ruthlessness' takes the pursuit of women by men as a typical example, but the pursuit also indicates that girls are also pursuing men in the same way. He can also use historical events to describe modernity, such as Du Fu's lover, making a scene in the palace, being obsessed, and also as if he once knew each other at the mouth of Wuyi Temple, allowing modernity to blend into the old poems. Sometimes, he is joking and saying something like a 'Snow Breakthrough Record,' but he also attaches importance to love ethics and writes a 'Brief Essay on Love Ethics,'" (words from the preface to the yellow shirt) In each section of this book, we can glimpse all kinds of beautiful relics worth remembering and envying. Love and strength are facts full of content. This theme is exceptionally wonderful.

As for his unique style, it can also be seen in several paragraphs pointed out in the preface to the yellow shirt, such as his ethereal, humorous, suggestive, and tender style. For example,

"Suddenly, the lights were dimmed. Who dimmed them? I don't know, maybe they like to sit in the dark room to see the light moon and silver light? Maybe it's so that no one can see whose face is blushing?" This paragraph in the section that was not described in the emotional part can be used as an example of an ethereal style. Also, for example, a paragraph at the place where charming eyes are full can be used as an example of humor and suggestion, "Ms. Cai was originally smiling, but now she is showing her teeth even more, and throwing down a flower again. I robbed her of throwing down all the flowers, but I no longer robbed her. The flower girl sang a good song and carried an empty basket."

Again, for example, "When your love cannot find a home, you feel that every girl in the universe has a charming charm. From the girl's body, there are all beautiful colors, all quiet sounds, the eyes are light green, the face is tender red, and everyone knows that the hair is dark and oily. Every sentence contains temptation and tenderness," how tender this is.

In the above paragraphs, we can see the general style and style of the author, but the reality of the content cannot be shown, because of the length of the article, I cannot copy a whole section, so that readers can see a little, but even if I did not copy it and give you an outline, however, if you like to know something about the general college life, I think it is worth buying a copy to read. If you are a member of the university, then you must read it, you can know whether your knowledge is as broad as the author's, and you can also find that there are such beautiful deeds embellishing your life circle.
